```ts
interface CalibrationAdmissionAuthorityRebuildTransactionV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-authority-rebuild-transaction-v1';
  readonly transactionId: string;
  readonly lockSha256: string;
  readonly invocationIntentId: string;
  readonly inputGenerationProposalId: string;
  readonly inputGenerationProposalSha256: string;
  readonly operation: 'create' | 'replace';
  readonly expectedCurrentState:
    | { readonly kind: 'absent' }
    | { readonly kind: 'existing'; readonly staticGenerationSha256: string };
  readonly recoveryNonce: string;
  readonly inputGenerationRelativePath: string;
  readonly staticGenerationStagingRelativePath: string;
  readonly authorityCurrentTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly authorityCurrentFinalRelativePath:
    'review/admission/authority/current.json';
  readonly sourceGenerationDirectories: readonly {
    readonly sourceId: string;
    readonly generationSha256: string;
    readonly artifactSetSha256: string;
    readonly generationStagingRelativePath: string;
    readonly generationFinalRelativePath: string;
    readonly generationsParentRelativePath: string;
    readonly priorGenerationRelativePath?: string;
    readonly currentPointerTemporaryRelativePath: string;
    readonly currentPointerFinalRelativePath: string;
  }[];
  readonly state:
    | { readonly phase: 'intent_fsynced' }
    | {
        readonly phase:
          | 'source_generation_directories_staged_fsynced'
          | 'source_generation_directories_promoted'
          | 'source_generation_parents_fsynced'
          | 'input_generation_fsynced'
          | 'overlap_generation_verified';
        readonly inputGenerationSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'primary_static_outputs_fsynced';
        readonly inputGenerationSha256: string;
        readonly overlapGenerationSha256: string;
        readonly primaryOutputSetSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'tool_receipt_indexed';
        readonly inputGenerationSha256: string;
        readonly overlapGenerationSha256: string;
        readonly primaryOutputSetSha256: string;
        readonly toolReceiptId: string;
        readonly toolReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase:
          | 'static_generation_staged_fsynced'
          | 'static_generation_promoted'
          | 'static_generations_parent_fsynced'
          | 'source_current_pointers_promoted'
          | 'authority_current_promoted'
          | 'output_directories_fsynced'
          | 'complete';
        readonly inputGenerationSha256: string;
        readonly overlapGenerationSha256: string;
        readonly primaryOutputSetSha256: string;
        readonly toolReceiptId: string;
        readonly toolReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
        readonly staticGenerationSha256: string;
        readonly staticGenerationRelativePath: string;
      };
  readonly transactionSha256: string;
}

// packages/core/src/calibration-admission.ts: no I/O, no runtime brand.

  | { readonly ok: false; readonly errors: readonly string[] };

interface CalibrationAdmissionWitnessPublicationTransactionV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-witness-publication-transaction-v1';
  readonly transactionId: string;
  readonly lockSha256: string;
  readonly operation: 'search_result' | 'witness_review';
  readonly gate: 'smoke' | 'canary';
  readonly invocationIntentId: string;
  readonly bundleSha256: string;
  readonly bundleBytes: number;
  readonly expectedRoutingReferenceState:
    | { readonly kind: 'absent' }
    | { readonly kind: 'existing'; readonly referenceSha256: string };
  readonly bundleTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly bundleFinalRelativePath: string;
  readonly completionTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly routingReferenceTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly routingReferenceFinalRelativePath: string;
  readonly recoveryNonce: string;
  readonly state:
    | { readonly phase: 'intent_fsynced' }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'required_tool_receipts_indexed';
        readonly requiredToolReceiptIds: readonly string[];
        readonly requiredToolReceiptSha256s: readonly string[];
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase:
          | 'bundle_staged_fsynced'
          | 'bundle_promoted'
          | 'output_directory_fsynced';
        readonly requiredToolReceiptIds: readonly string[];
        readonly requiredToolReceiptSha256s: readonly string[];
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'publication_tool_receipt_started';
        readonly requiredToolReceiptIds: readonly string[];
        readonly requiredToolReceiptSha256s: readonly string[];
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase:
          | 'publication_tool_receipt_indexed'
          | 'completion_staged_fsynced'
          | 'completion_promoted'
          | 'completion_directory_fsynced'
          | 'routing_reference_staged_fsynced'
          | 'routing_reference_promoted'
          | 'projections_directory_fsynced';
        readonly requiredToolReceiptIds: readonly string[];
        readonly requiredToolReceiptSha256s: readonly string[];
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
        readonly publicationToolReceiptId: string;
        readonly publicationToolReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
        readonly publicationCompletionSha256: string;
        readonly publicationCompletionFinalRelativePath: string;
        readonly nextRoutingReferenceSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'complete';
        readonly requiredToolReceiptIds: readonly string[];
        readonly requiredToolReceiptSha256s: readonly string[];
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
        readonly publicationCompletionSha256: string;
        readonly publicationCompletionFinalRelativePath: string;
        readonly nextRoutingReferenceSha256: string;
        readonly completion:
          | {
              readonly kind: 'search_result';
              readonly searchToolReceiptId: string;
              readonly searchToolReceiptSha256: string;
              readonly publicationToolReceiptId: string;
              readonly publicationToolReceiptSha256: string;
            }
          | {
              readonly kind: 'witness_review';
              readonly publicationToolReceiptId: string;
              readonly publicationToolReceiptSha256: string;
            };
      };
  readonly transactionSha256: string;
}

declare const verifiedReadyAdmissionCensusBrand: unique symbol; // module-private
type VerifiedReadyAdmissionCensusV1 = Readonly<{
  readonly context: VerifiedAdmissionContextV1;
  readonly census: CalibrationAdmissionCensusV103;
  readonly witnessReviewBundle: CalibrationAdmissionWitnessReviewBundleV1;
  readonly [verifiedReadyAdmissionCensusBrand]: true;
}>;

declare function verifyReadyAdmissionCensus(
  root: string,
  context: VerifiedAdmissionContextV1,
  censusInput: unknown,
  witnessReviewBundleInput: unknown,
): Promise<
  | { readonly ok: true; readonly ready: VerifiedReadyAdmissionCensusV1 }
  | { readonly ok: false; readonly errors: readonly string[] }
>;
```

`rebuild:pre-witness` owns source-generation publication; callers provide only
validated proposals and generation-local artifact inputs. Under the rebuild
lock, it creates each transaction-bound staged directory, writes and rehashes
the complete generation, no-clobber promotes every directory to the exact
transaction-recorded hash-named final path, and fsyncs every distinct source
`generations/` parent before promoting any source-current pointer. The journal
records all 329 create-mode entries (or the exact replacement set), including
generation/artifact hashes and staged/final/parent/prior paths. Recovery uses
only that closed set: a prefix-promoted genesis or replacement is rolled
forward only when every directory revalidates, otherwise transaction-owned
staging is removed and no pointer advances. Orphan discovery is forbidden.

`VerifiedAdmissionContextV1` is not persisted and has no Core JSON Schema.
`pre-witness-bundle.json` **is** persisted, but the production builder and
verifier begin from exactly one mutable root:
`review/admission/authority/current.json`. They schema-validate and self-hash
that pointer, resolve its exact immutable static generation, then resolve that
generation's input generation, source generations, overlap generation, and
every hash-pinned artifact without directory discovery. The fixed Section 4
files are optional, byte-verified projections only; they never override or
supplement the immutable generation graph. The resolved graph includes the
complete tool-authority index/generation chain and its content-addressed
objects, and verification requires byte-identical recomposition. An unindexed
tool/acquisition artifact, orphan generation, pointer/path mismatch, or flat
projection not equal to its pinned artifact is invalid.
SlopBrick keeps both the module-private symbol and a module-private
`WeakSet<object>` runtime registry. The factory canonicalizes and deep-freezes
the context, inserts that exact object into the registry only after every Core
schema/semantic/reference check, receipt/profile check, exact current register/
review ID-set equality (329 only in generation 0), acquisition-delta chain,
CAS byte rehash, complete materialization revalidation, and cross-ledger set/
hash check passes. It opens the exact contained admission-record JSONL itself,
recomputes every canonical record hash and both stream/set hashes, and stores a
private immutable `recordId -> record/source/decision` map. Caller-supplied
records are never disposition authority. `deriveAdmissionDisposition` first checks
`verifiedContexts.has(context)` and throws a typed invalid-context error for a
cast, clone, deserialized object, or object from another module instance.
Core never imports this type, never derives a disposition, and never performs
I/O; it validates only durable artifacts.

Context construction runs under `admission-context-v1`, exposes no network
client or process spawn surface, clears proxy/credential/askpass variables,
and reads evidence only from contained CAS paths plus materialization bytes
through the already-reviewed offline release/Git resolver. Missing bytes fail
closed. The exported production factory constructs its no-follow contained
filesystem and resolvers internally; dependency injection is module-private
test support and is not exported from the package. A malicious fake filesystem
therefore cannot mint a production brand. The context hash binds the policy,
its exact smoke/canary witness-policy expansions,
record stream and each canonical record hash, every task-scoped intent/profile/
receipt, acquisition authorization/receipt/delta, payload set, evidence/
materialization receipt, pre-witness blind receipt, temporal attestation, every
current source review, and every authority ledger. Semantic target partitioning
rejects any witness-target assignment, decision, blind receipt, search receipt,
or witness-review object inside the pre-witness bundle.

Each gate first persists a search-result bundle containing its exact witness or
certificate, search receipt, and the gate-specific search invocation intents/tool
receipts needed to resolve that result. A witness-review bundle is persisted
separately only for a witness and may contain only that gate's exact
witness-target graph; it embeds the search-result bundle plus two distinct
regeneration intent/receipt/witness proofs and one constraint-check intent/
receipt/result proof. None of those search/
review receipts may appear in or influence the pre-witness context hash.

These two bundles are the sole complete witness authorities. Each is canonical,
no-clobber published at the hash-derived contained path
`review/admission/witnesses/$GATE/{search-results|witness-reviews}/$BUNDLE_SHA256.json`
under the per-gate lock/transaction; there is no mutable witness current
pointer. The exploded witness, receipt, assignment, and reviewer files are
optional verified projections and cannot be discovered as authority. The search
action indexes its result-producing tool receipt before finalizing the bundle
that embeds it. This computation mutates no witness path and opens no witness
lock/transaction; only after the receipt is indexed and the complete bundle
hash exists may publication begin. The CLI then creates a second distinct intent/receipt for
`witness:publish-search`; its canonical argv/input/output projection is the
complete bundle, and that external publication receipt is recorded only in the
hash-addressed publication completion, never only in the transient journal.
The two intent IDs and receipt IDs must differ and may not replay one
another. Witness-review publication freezes the already-complete bundle
first, indexes its external publication receipt afterward, and never inserts
that future receipt into the bundle. After receipt indexing, each publisher
no-clobber writes/fsyncs
`publication-completions/$COMPLETION_SHA256.json`, binding gate/kind, bundle,
publication intent/receipt, required result/review receipts, tool-authority
index, parent transaction, and the complete self-hashed `completed_fsynced`
nested handoff object. It must be byte-identical to the immutable handoff twin
before transient cleanup. This is the durable
parent completion marker required before journal cleanup. A successful transaction fsyncs the
hash-addressed object/directory and removes/fsyncs transaction before lock.
Recovery validates the exact temp/final hashes and required tool receipts,
rolls forward only complete same-byte output or removes only its own temp, and
never deletes an unknown bundle. Same-hash writers are idempotent; different-
hash writers may both persist, but no bundle is selected until a later census
pins its exact kind/path/hash.

After each successful publication, the same transaction writes the matching
fixed `projections/{search-reference|witness-review-reference}.json` as a
schema-valid routing reference that binds both bundle and immutable publication
completion paths/hashes, then fsyncs the projections directory. It is not
a current pointer and cannot authorize a bundle: every consumer must validate
the reference, require both hash-derived paths, and reopen/rehash the complete
bundle, completion, tool-index generation, and publication receipt. The census
persists those exact bundle and completion refs so historical verification
never needs the mutable routing projection. Recovery may restore/replace only its transaction-bound
reference bytes. The lock/transaction intent binds only the expected reference
state (`absent` or exact prior `referenceSha256`); the next reference hash is
derived only after the future publication receipt/completion exists and appears
only in that post-receipt transaction state. Under the lock, pre-completion
recovery accepts/restores only the exact expected prior state, while post-
completion recovery may accept/promote only the exact next reference. An
unknown/stale reference, occupied different-byte next path, or missing prior is
a recovery error, never permission
to scan the bundle directory.

An exact bundle already referenced with the same completion is idempotent and
creates no new transaction/receipt. A same-bundle publication with a different
intent while that reference is current is rejected; after a different bundle
has replaced the routing reference, switching back creates a new completion
under its own hash and CAS-updates the reference without overwriting history.

There is no separate witness-review proposal contract. The proposal bytes are
the exact complete `CalibrationAdmissionWitnessReviewBundleV1` stored under
`proposals/$BUNDLE_SHA256.json`; `PROPOSAL_SHA256`, `bundle.bundleSha256`, and
the canonical file SHA must be equal. `witness:publish-review` reopens and
validates those exact bytes and the embedded search bundle before starting its
publication transaction. Any incomplete draft lives outside the canonical
proposal path and is not accepted.

`verifyReadyAdmissionCensus` reconstructs
and revalidates the pre-witness context, eligibility snapshot, witness, search
receipt, two calibration decisions, post-decision blind receipt, witness-review
receipt, and final census links before registering the exact frozen ready
object in a second private WeakSet. A plain schema-valid census, a cast, a
bundle for the other gate, or a bundle containing source/record/temporal
decisions can never satisfy the manifest builder.
Adapter audit values in a record remain claims for mismatch diagnostics;
authoritative syntax/scaffold, materialization, overlap, privacy, secret,
family, pair, and split results come from the branded context. Any self-
declared `pass` that disagrees with a ledger derives
`adapter_audit_mismatch` plus the authoritative blocker.

### 5.4 Per-code-unit admission record

```ts
type AdmissionLabel =
  | 'verified_ai'
  | 'verified_human'
  | 'mixed'
  | 'quarantine';

type HumanEditStatus = 'none' | 'light' | 'substantial' | 'unknown';

type ModelRevisionEvidence =
  | { readonly status: 'pinned'; readonly value: string }
  | {
      readonly status: 'provider_not_exposed';
      readonly hostedServiceProductId: string;
      readonly provider: string;
      readonly modelAlias: string;
      readonly generationDate: string;
      readonly providerVersioningEvidenceId: string;
      readonly acceptingReviewerDecisionIds: readonly [string, string];
    };

interface CalibrationAdmissionRecordV103 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-record-v1';
  readonly recordId: string;              // canonical SHA-256-derived ID
  readonly materialSourceId: string;
  readonly aggregateSourceIds: readonly string[];
  readonly sourceReviewSha256: string;
  readonly logicalUnitId: string;
  readonly locator:
    | {
        readonly kind: 'git_file';
        readonly materializationId: string;
        readonly normalizedPath: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'release_archive_file';
        readonly materializationId: string;
        readonly normalizedPath: string; // relative to reviewed rootPrefix
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'record_container';
        readonly materializationId: string;
        readonly containerSha256: string;
        readonly rowKey: string;
        readonly field: string;
      };
  readonly contentSha256: string;
  readonly contentBytes: number;
  readonly language: string;
  readonly stratum: 'production' | 'test' | 'generated' | 'vendor' |
    'minified' | 'example' | 'other';
  readonly proposedLabel: AdmissionLabel;
  readonly authorship:
    | {
        readonly kind: 'generator_record';
        readonly evidenceIds: readonly string[];
        readonly generatorProvider: string;
        readonly model: string;
        readonly modelRevision: ModelRevisionEvidence;
        readonly generatorSource:
          | { readonly kind: 'source_commit'; readonly commitSha: string }
          | { readonly kind: 'hosted_service' };
        readonly promptTaskId: string;
        readonly promptSha256: string;
        readonly outputSha256: string;
        readonly generatedAt: string;
        readonly humanEditStatus: HumanEditStatus;
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'benchmark_attestation';
        readonly evidenceIds: readonly string[];
        readonly benchmarkId: string;
        readonly benchmarkVersion: string;
        readonly exactUnitBinding: string;
        readonly attestedAuthorship: 'ai_generated' | 'human_written';
        readonly generator?: {
          readonly generatorProvider: string;
          readonly model: string;
          readonly modelRevision: ModelRevisionEvidence;
          readonly promptTaskId: string;
          readonly promptSha256: string;
          readonly outputSha256: string;
          readonly generatedAt: string;
        };
        readonly humanEditStatus: HumanEditStatus | 'not_applicable';
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'repository_attestation';
        readonly evidenceIds: readonly string[];
        readonly scope: 'file' | 'directory' | 'repository';
        readonly generatorFamily: string;
        readonly humanEditStatus: HumanEditStatus;
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'historical_inference';
        readonly evidenceIds: readonly string[];
        readonly blobSha: string;
        readonly introducedAt: string;
        readonly lastChangedAt: string;
        readonly cutoff: '2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z';
        readonly temporalAttestationId?: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'unproven_claim';
        readonly evidenceIds: readonly string[];
        readonly declaredClaim: 'ai' | 'human' | 'mixed' | 'unknown';
        readonly missingFields: readonly string[];
      };
  readonly claimedLineage: {
    readonly familyId: string;
    readonly pairGroupId?: string;
    readonly originRecordId: string;
    readonly exactClusterId: string;
    readonly nearClusterId: string;
  };
  readonly claimedAudits: {
    readonly syntax: 'pass' | 'fail' | 'unsupported';
    readonly scaffoldByteShare: number;
    readonly privacy: 'pass' | 'review' | 'fail';
    readonly secrets: 'pass' | 'review' | 'fail';
    readonly exactOverlap: 'pass' | 'fail';
    readonly nearOverlap: 'pass' | 'fail' | 'unsupported';
    readonly familyLeakage: 'pass' | 'fail';
    readonly pairIntegrity: 'pass' | 'fail' | 'not_applicable';
  };
  readonly reviewerDecisionIds: readonly string[];
  readonly declaredDisposition:
    | 'eligible_gold'
    | 'eligible_sensitivity'
    | 'mixed_evaluation'
    | 'quarantine';
  readonly rejectionReasons: readonly AdmissionReason[];
}
```

The record ID is the lowercase SHA-256 of canonical JSON containing exactly
`materialSourceId`, `logicalUnitId`, `locator`, `contentSha256`, `contentBytes`,
and `language`. Source-review decisions, family/cluster assignments, reviewer
decisions, and mutable prose do not change code-unit identity; their hashes
still bind the census and invalidate a stale eligibility result.
For a container without a publisher item ID, `rowKey` is
`$CONTAINER_SHA256:$ZERO_BASED_ROW_INDEX`; the `field` then distinguishes
`human_src`, `llm_src`, `Code`, or another schema-approved code field. Row
order is therefore bound to immutable container bytes.
An original unit sets `originRecordId = recordId`; a derived/paraphrased unit
points to the exact source unit's record ID. Singleton exact and near clusters
still receive stable IDs. Near-cluster IDs are connected components of the
verified `>= 0.80` edge graph, not LSH bucket IDs.
An AI `benchmark_attestation` requires its `generator` object,
`humanEditStatus != not_applicable`, and an output hash matching the record. A
human benchmark attestation omits `generator` and uses
`humanEditStatus = not_applicable`; its proposed label must match
`attestedAuthorship`.
`unproven_claim` exists to preserve a countable intake record without
fabricating complete authorship fields. It always derives
`authorship_unproven` and can never be eligible.
`claimedLineage` and `claimedAudits` never authorize eligibility; the verified
lineage/overlap/privacy/materialization ledgers do. Eligible evidence IDs must
resolve through the index and verified receipts. Local-unpublished evidence
can bind current facts honestly but never satisfies an immutable gate.
A `provider_not_exposed` revision is not a bare exception: the provider/model,
generation date, immutable official versioning-contract evidence ID, and two
distinct accepting reviewer decisions plus their post-decision blind receipt
must all resolve in the context. Missing
or contradicted evidence derives `generator_revision_missing`. The controlled
GPT-5 cohort is not grandfathered and remains quarantined until this exception
is independently accepted.

### 5.5 Structured independent admission decision

```ts
type AdmissionDisposition =
  | 'eligible_gold'
  | 'eligible_sensitivity'
  | 'mixed_evaluation'
  | 'quarantine';

interface CalibrationAdmissionDecisionV103 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-decision-v1';
  readonly decisionId: string;
  readonly target:
    | { readonly kind: 'source'; readonly sourceId: string }
    | { readonly kind: 'record'; readonly recordId: string }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'provider_revision_exception';
        readonly recordId: string;
        readonly providerVersioningEvidenceId: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'witness';
        readonly witnessSha256: string;
        readonly eligibilitySnapshotSha256: string;
        readonly verifiedContextSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'temporal_attestation';
        readonly temporalAttestationId: string;
        readonly exactBlobOrContentSha256: string;
      };
  readonly reviewerId: string;
  readonly reviewerRoles: readonly (
    | 'authorship'
    | 'rights'
    | 'leakage_privacy'
    | 'calibration'
    | 'provenance'
  )[];
  readonly evidenceIds: readonly string[];
  readonly blindAssignmentId: string;
  readonly adjudicatesDecisionIds?: readonly [string, string];
  readonly result:
    | {
        readonly kind: 'admission';
        readonly proposedLabel: AdmissionLabel;
        readonly humanEditStatus: HumanEditStatus | 'not_applicable';
        readonly disposition: AdmissionDisposition;
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'provider_revision_exception';
        readonly decision: 'accepted' | 'rejected';
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'temporal_attestation';
        readonly decision: 'accepted' | 'rejected';
      }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'witness';
        readonly decision: 'approved' | 'rejected';
      };
  readonly reasons: readonly AdmissionReason[];
  readonly decidedAt: string;
}
```

`decisionId` is derived from the canonical decision without `decisionId`.
Reviewer decisions sort by canonical target, then `reviewerId`; all IDs and
roles are sorted and unique. Two decisions for an eligible source/record use
distinct reviewer IDs, each binds the exact evidence set, and together cover
authorship and rights; the rights reviewer must explicitly approve the rights
evidence IDs used by the source or asset. Each blind decision references only
its pre-existing blind assignment. The post-decision blind receipt references
the two completed decisions and proves peer material stayed hidden; decisions
never reference that later receipt or each other. Disagreement requires a
third adjudicator whose decision links exactly the two prior IDs; it is not
rewritten into agreement. An adjudication decision uses a distinct assignment
whose evidence includes both sealed decisions and does not retroactively alter
their receipt. `decidedAt` is reviewer evidence, not census-generated time.
A witness decision is created only after the witness exists, binds the exact
witness/snapshot/context triple also named by its blind assignment and later
witness-review receipt, uses `reviewerRoles = ['calibration']`, and has
`result.kind = 'witness'` with an explicit `approved|rejected` value. A
temporal-attestation decision uses only the independent `provenance` role and
an explicit `accepted|rejected` result; two accepted decisions plus their
matching post-decision blind receipt must resolve over that exact attestation/
content hash. Provider exceptions likewise use their own explicit result.
Source/record decisions use only `result.kind = 'admission'`.
Semantic validation rejects every target/result/role mismatch. Witness and
temporal decisions cannot adjudicate or substitute for source/record
authorship or rights decisions, and an approved witness-review receipt is
derivable only from two matching `witness: approved` decisions.

### 5.6 Rejection/quarantine reason vocabulary

The schema permits only these sorted, unique reason codes:

```ts
type AdmissionReason =
  | 'source_unregistered'
  | 'source_revision_mutable'
  | 'source_bytes_unbound'
  | 'source_inventory_open'
  | 'source_inventory_mismatch'
  | 'aggregate_material_conservation_failed'
  | 'material_source_conflict'
  | 'evidence_unresolved'
  | 'evidence_receipt_stale'
  | 'record_container_projection_unsupported'
  | 'materialization_unsupported'
  | 'materialization_unverified'
  | 'materialization_receipt_stale'
  | 'license_absent'
  | 'license_scope_ambiguous'
  | 'analysis_use_unresolved'
  | 'analysis_use_denied'
  | 'redistribution_unresolved'
  | 'redistribution_denied'
  | 'third_party_rights_unresolved'
  | 'authorship_unproven'
  | 'generator_identity_missing'
  | 'generator_revision_missing'
  | 'prompt_binding_missing'
  | 'output_binding_mismatch'
  | 'human_edit_unknown'
  | 'human_edit_substantial'
  | 'human_provenance_missing'
  | 'historical_cutoff_failed'
  | 'historical_attestation_missing'
  | 'historical_graph_incomplete'
  | 'mixed_authorship'
  | 'family_unknown'
  | 'pair_incomplete'
  | 'pair_content_unsafe'
  | 'exact_cross_polarity_overlap'
  | 'near_cross_polarity_overlap'
  | 'unpaired_family_cross_polarity'
  | 'split_leakage'
  | 'lineage_ledger_incomplete'
  | 'overlap_universe_incomplete'
  | 'overlap_authority_incomplete'
  | 'privacy_ledger_incomplete'
  | 'quality_ledger_incomplete'
  | 'adapter_audit_mismatch'
  | 'privacy_high_confidence'
  | 'secret_high_confidence'
  | 'privacy_review_unresolved'
  | 'syntax_invalid'
  | 'language_normalizer_unsupported'
  | 'scaffold_dominant'
  | 'trivial_or_inert_target'
  | 'duplicate_record'
  | 'blind_review_receipt_missing'
  | 'witness_review_receipt_missing'
  | 'review_incomplete'
  | 'review_disagreement'
  | 'source_wide_quarantine';
```

The census counts record-level reasons by source and proposed label, and
source-wide reasons by source. It never multiplies one source blocker into an
invented file-level polarity result. Adding or changing a reason requires
`v10.3-admission-record-v2`; do not silently change v1.

### 5.7 Global universe, authoritative ledgers, and exact witnesses

```ts
          | 'current_output_projections_promoted'
          | 'current_generation_promoted'

          | 'complete';
        readonly primaryOutputSetSha256: string;

        readonly toolReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;

        readonly generationDirectoryFinalRelativePath: string;
        readonly artifactSetSha256: string;

    readonly verifiedHuman: number;
```
