- [ ] **Step 1: write red Core and SlopBrick tests**

  Core tests cover every schema/self-hash/reference invariant. SlopBrick tests
  prove the smoke/canary witness-policy objects are the unique lossless
  deterministic expansion of the durable policy and reject omitted/changed
  constraints. They create a contained CAS root and cover `wx` creation, same-byte idempotence,
  different-byte collision, mandatory intent/temporary/link publication,
  interruption after every write/link/unlink/file-fsync/directory-fsync,
  deletion/substitution,

  rejection of a CAS copy for already-owned bytes, local-unpublished
  ineligibility, symlink/path escape, wrong media type/byte count, missing/wrong profile,

  deserialized context must fail the module-private WeakSet brand check.
  CAS tests freeze the primary-completion object before either nested child,
  mutate every projection field, and prove the indexed final envelope—not a
  later transaction self-hash—is the durable marker for cleanup recovery.
  Tool-authority tests race unrelated action intents/receipts, crash every
  index/object/fsync/unlink phase, and prove explicit recovery preserves every
  immutable object and exactly one ordered index chain. Cover absent-current

  paths, empty generation-0 create, generation-1 evidence replace, stale-parent

  lock-directory fsync but before transaction intent exists; the lock's

  the parent fields, reject an extra/missing/reordered base or intent-authority

- [ ] **Step 1: write red tests with a self-contained 329-source fixture**

  Generate 12 aggregate/top-level plus 317 material-leaf register entries in
  the test itself. Assert exact source-review set equality, material ownership,

  the one-way parent -> delta -> next register -> generation receipt order and
  reject any delta that embeds its future register/receipt hash or any register
  entry that embeds its future delta ID.

  generation CAS, separate post-proposal approval, content-addressed artifact
  set, and current pointer; mutate
  any review/decision/record artifact without changing its filename and reject.
  Every artifact kind has an exact allowed contained path/schema/media
  semantics; kind/path substitution is rejected. A two-source delta must bind
  every field of the shared added-source shape; deleting or swapping the second
  source's generation/materialization hash is a required mutation failure.
  Prove the exact proposal -> approval -> generation -> delta -> next-register
  graph and reject an approval embedded in or created before its proposal.
  Generation-path fixtures reject an outer generation hash/root path in a
  `generation_local` receipt, a non-hash-derived root CAS path, and any prior
  generation that becomes unreadable after current-pointer replacement.
  Register-publication fault tests cover one- and two-source create/replace
  transactions at every source staged-directory fsync, whole-directory no-
  clobber rename, per-source `generations/` parent fsync, source-current CAS,
  register-generation write, and cleanup boundary. Recovery re-opens the exact
  prior and next source directories from transaction-recorded paths, handles a
  partially promoted two-source set without mixing generations, and never
  treats a flat path or directory-discovered orphan as authority.
  The register suite also kills after lock-file and lock-directory fsync before
  transaction creation and proves `register:recover --from-lock` recomputes the
  intended transaction identity from the lock envelope alone.

  Create the blind assignment first, decisions second, and post-decision
  receipt third. Prove no decision contains peer/receipt IDs and mutate each
  edge. Review-sample tests recompute every selection/presentation key and
  stratum count; decision-ledger tests require exact JSONL hashes and ID-set
  equality with no missing, extra, duplicated, or cross-source object.
  Temporal tests require an exact externally observed content hash,
  verified evidence receipts, `observedAt <= 2020-01-01`, complete Git graph,
  and two independent blinded provenance reviewers plus their post-decision
  receipt. Git dates alone must derive sensitivity,
  never gold.
  A plain/cast/cloned/deserialized evidence bundle must fail the Task 1A
  WeakSet handoff before any source count is emitted.

- [ ] **Step 2: implement Core validators and SlopBrick review authority**

  `source:census` consumes `VerifiedAdmissionEvidenceContextV1` plus register/reviews/records/
  decisions, writes no file, and emits canonical per-source registered,
  represented, unrepresented, and quarantine counts. It cannot accept or
  construct static-ledger/final-context authority from later slices.

  `census:current-hash` first refuses any live census journal, reopens and
  schema/semantic-validates the canonical census and sidecar, recomputes its
  canonical hash, compares the sidecar, and only then emits that hash. It never
  accepts a caller-provided hash, diagnostic `shasum`, or history artifact.
  Implement `witness:search`, `witness:publish-search`, `witness:publish-review`, and
  `witness:recover-publication` in the same CLI. `witness:search` invokes Task

  authority into one search-result bundle. The orchestration then invokes
  `witness:publish-search` under a distinct intent/receipt to no-clobber publish
  that bundle.
  `witness:publish-review` accepts only the already-complete schema-valid review
  bundle and publishes its external action receipt after the bundle bytes;
  neither action writes a mutable current pointer. `census` accepts only exact
  hash-derived bundle and publication-completion paths and stores all four
  relative-path/hash values per authority.

  ```bash
      --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
      --publication-proposal review/admission/acquisitions/proposals/genesis-empty-index.json \

  )"
  ```

  After Step 1 has prepared and independently hash-checked the complete genesis

  create mode. It freezes the input generation, runs/publishes the bound

  ```bash
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- rebuild:pre-witness \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --input-generation-proposal review/admission/authority/proposals/genesis-input.json \
    --operation create \
    --expect-current-absent \
    --tool-profile admission-static-ledgers-v1 \
    --require-real-scale-receipt

    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --tool-profile admission-static-ledgers-v1 \
    --require-real-scale-receipt

    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --tool-profile admission-context-v1 \
    --require-real-scale-receipt
  ```

  All 452,382 initial rows plus any already-registered new candidates must

  complete. Run overlap verification twice and require byte-identical hashes.

  Assert the create transaction is gone, every source current pointer resolves

- [ ] **Step 4: reproduce byte identity**

  Render twice without filesystem mutation from identical canonical inputs and
  compare the complete canonical stdout. Every persisted result/search hash is
  contained in that rendering; `verify` separately reopens the bound files:

  ```bash
  SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    witness:search --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --gate smoke --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    witness:search --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --gate canary --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  FIRST=$(mktemp)
  SECOND=$(mktemp)
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- census --stdout \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --smoke-search-bundle "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-bundle-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-bundle "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-bundle-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1 > "$FIRST"
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- census --stdout \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --smoke-search-bundle "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-bundle-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-bundle "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-bundle-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1 > "$SECOND"
  shasum -a 256 "$FIRST" "$SECOND"
  cmp "$FIRST" "$SECOND"
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- verify \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1 \
    --census review/eligible-census-v10.3.json
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4: regenerate census after each accepted source decision**

  Never combine two source changes before observing their individual effect on
  eligible and rejection counts. A review/audit proposal is not authority until
  the following full generation order succeeds: source generation + admission
  records/record-stream/overlap-universe input generation -> overlap generation
  -> privacy/quality/lineage -> pre-witness bundle/static generation -> branded
  context -> gate search-result bundles -> census.

  ```bash
  cd /Users/cheng/platform
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- rebuild:pre-witness \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --input-generation-proposal "$INPUT_GENERATION_PROPOSAL" \
    --operation replace \
    --expected-current-static-generation-sha256 "$CURRENT_STATIC_GENERATION_SHA256" \
    --tool-profile admission-static-ledgers-v1 \
    --require-real-scale-receipt
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- context:verify \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --tool-profile admission-context-v1 \
    --require-real-scale-receipt
  SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    witness:search --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --gate smoke --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    witness:search --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --gate canary --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CURRENT_SHA=$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    census:current-hash \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --census review/eligible-census-v10.3.json \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1)
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- census \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --smoke-search-bundle "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-bundle-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-bundle "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-bundle-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1 \
    --out review/eligible-census-v10.3.json \
    --replace-if-current-sha "$CURRENT_SHA"
  ```

  `census:current-hash` schema-validates and hashes the exact current file;
  diagnostic `shasum` output never supplies a CAS token. On any interrupted
  rebuild, run `static-authority:recover` with either transaction ID or
  `--from-lock`, plus nonce and no-live-writer acknowledgement, before retrying.

- [ ] **Step 3: human-negative source review**

  Start with HumanEval. If still deficient, review no more than five existing
  legacy-human repositories in the first historical-inference batch. Hash and
  review exact blobs; do not count the remainder of a repository. For each
  gold candidate, locate and preflight an independent timestamped
  archive/package-registry/release-transparency observation that binds the
  exact blob/content no later than 2020-01-01, but record only its exact URL,
  expected hash/bytes/media type, rights, and proposed evidence-acquisition
  authorization in this preflight. Task 7 performs any actual CAS acquisition
  and only then may two independent provenance reviewers seal decisions over
  the byte-verified receipt. A complete Git history
  without that external observation is sensitivity-only. Each reviewed
  repository leaf is already a generation-0 material source: CAS-replace its
  existing quarantine review for the same source ID/register-entry hash before
  creating records, while retaining its one existing checkout; do not
  register or count the unreviewed remainder merely because it shares a parent
  directory. The batch directory contains reusable audit code only; it is not a
  source ID and emits no batch authority. Invoke the adapter once for each
  selected exact existing `repositoryId` (one required, at most five), and
  require each singular proposal's `sourceId`/register-entry hash to match that
  leaf. `source:audit-node` rejects an ID absent from the current register and
  must not create a directory for it.

  ```bash
  cd /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3
  : "${HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_ID_1:?set exact existing repositoryId}"
  HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_IDS=(
    "$HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_ID_1"
    "${HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_ID_2:-}"
    "${HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_ID_3:-}"
    "${HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_ID_4:-}"
    "${HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_ID_5:-}"
  )
  SEEN_SOURCE_IDS=" "
  for SOURCE_ID in "${HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_IDS[@]}"; do
    test -n "$SOURCE_ID" || continue
    case "$SOURCE_ID" in
      *[!a-z0-9._-]*) echo "invalid repositoryId: $SOURCE_ID" >&2; exit 2 ;;
    esac
    case "$SEEN_SOURCE_IDS" in
      *" $SOURCE_ID "*) echo "duplicate repositoryId: $SOURCE_ID" >&2; exit 2 ;;
    esac
    SEEN_SOURCE_IDS="$SEEN_SOURCE_IDS$SOURCE_ID "
    node review/admission/sources/historical-human-batch-1/test-audit-historical-human.mjs \
      --source-id "$SOURCE_ID"
  done
  cd /Users/cheng/platform
  for SOURCE_ID in "${HISTORICAL_HUMAN_SOURCE_IDS[@]}"; do
    test -n "$SOURCE_ID" || continue
    corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- source:audit-node \
      --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
      --source-id "$SOURCE_ID" \
      --adapter review/admission/sources/historical-human-batch-1/audit-historical-human.mjs \
      --tool-profile admission-source-node-v1 \
      --out "review/admission/sources/$SOURCE_ID/proposals/audit.json.next"
  done
  ```

### Task 7 — implement hardened acquisition, then take pull/no-pull decision

**Files:**

- Consume the already-reviewed Task 1A/1B evidence/source acquisition,
  round-lock/transaction/receipt, and register-delta Core contracts; do not
  introduce a competing shape.
- Create: `packages/slopbrick/src/calibration/v103/admission-acquisition.ts`
- Modify: `packages/slopbrick/scripts/cal/v103-admission.ts`
- Create: `packages/slopbrick/tests/calibration/v103-admission-acquisition.test.ts`
- Modify: `packages/slopbrick/tests/calibration/v103-admission-cli-e2e.test.ts`
- Modify external admission evidence and source register only after owner
  authorization.
- Modify the platform admission evidence doc with the reviewed decision.

- [ ] **Step 1: write failing authorization/acquisition tests**

  Cover every Section 9 schema/containment/network/config/hook/filter/tree/
  limit/interruption/receipt case before mutation code. Include separate Git
  unbounded-transport acknowledgement and release hard-stream-cap fixtures;
  exact-origin DNS/socket capability denial; redirect/private-address/proxy/
  credential attempts; and cross-use of Git/release tool profiles.
  Cover exact-URL evidence acquisition separately, including media/hash/byte
  mismatch, redirect/DNS/peer binding, CAS crash recovery, and proof that it
  cannot materialize source/archive bytes. Assert the exact acyclic
  authorization -> payload descriptor/indexed intent/wx reservation ->
  transaction -> receipts -> envelope
  construction order and mutate each edge. Kill after CAS publication but
  before each observation/receipt/payload/envelope/index publication and after
  transaction unlink/directory fsync; `evidence:recover` must be idempotent and
  never refetch a consumed one-use authorization. Same-authorization concurrent
  acquisition must make the loser exit before
  DNS; recovery of a reserved/partially consumed authorization never refetches.
  Kill before/after transaction-intent fsync and reservation `wx` before DNS;
  recovery must clean an unreserved loser transaction or resume only the exact
  winning reservation.
  Cover a mixed-transport two-source round, sum-of-maxima >5 GiB rejection
  before DNS, two concurrent rounds,
  crash after every round-lock/transaction/promotion/fsync boundary, and
  all-or-nothing register publication. Register-generation fault tests include
  one/two source-generation staged-directory fsync, whole-directory no-clobber
  promotion, each source `generations/` parent fsync, a partial first-of-two
  promotion, generation-receipt/global-tool-authority publication, source-
  current and current-register-last CAS, transaction/lock unlink plus directory
  fsync, concurrent writers, and idempotent recovery after each boundary. Every
  fault re-opens exact prior/next source directories from the journal and never
  discovers or removes an orphan.
  For each source, separately fault the pre-DNS
  `source-intent-authority:$SOURCE_ID` tool-index publication and the post-
  output `source-tool-receipt:$SOURCE_ID` publication; DNS is unreachable until
  every source intent is indexed, and source output remains solely in the round
  transaction rather than a fabricated per-source child transaction.
  Source construction-order tests prove authorization -> stable transaction
  primary output/child tool receipt -> materialization receipt -> source
  acquisition receipt -> round receipt -> acquisition-index/evidence bundle ->
  blind review/source generation -> register delta, and reject every backward
  or future hash edge.
  Authorization-only acquisition-index publication gets its own two-writer and
  every-phase crash suite; `acquisition:recover-publication` must restore or
  advance the exact index generation and preserve every unknown object.
  Both round and acquisition-publication suites kill after lock-file/lock-
  directory fsync before transaction creation; their `--from-lock` recoveries
  derive the intended transaction ID from the fixed lock and never require an
  unwritten ID.
  Prove acquired-but-unreviewed and acquired-but-rejected sources remain absent
  from source generations/register deltas. Mutate post-download closed
  inventory, rights/authorship/label decisions, blind receipt, separate source-
  generation approval, stable materialization receipt, and either source of a
  two-source delta. Verify the immutable materialization JSONL generation is
  sorted/unique, acquisition-indexed, set-equal to the evidence bundle, and its
  fixed projection is byte-identical; deletion/substitution/reorder fails.

- [ ] **Step 2: implement the offline-default evidence and round CLIs**

  `register:{publish-round,recover}`. Use injected
  `spawn`/transport/filesystem boundaries and Git tree plumbing internally;
  never shell interpolation or `git checkout`. No generic fetch API is
  exported.

- [ ] **Step 5: rank no more than three preflight candidates**

  Use this order: already-reviewed remediation, controlled expansion with
  complete generation records, public benchmark with item-level evidence,
  then repository attestation. Score expected eligible yield, language/family
  diversity, rights clarity, materialization support, transfer size, and review
  cost. Do not rank by stars or dataset size.

- [ ] **Step 6: request explicit owner authorization**

  Name exact source(s), commits/assets, declared bytes, rights basis, and
  expected deficit coverage. No authorization means stop with a valid census,
  not a blocked/partial acquisition.

- [ ] **Step 7: acquire exact evidence and at most two sources, then rerun all gates**

  First acquire only approved provenance evidence needed by a reviewed current
  candidate. Reverify its indexed CAS bytes, create the exact temporal-
  attestation or provider-exception target, preassign two eligible reviewers,
  seal both blinded decisions, and publish the post-decision blind receipt.
  CAS-stage a replacement source-review/admission-record generation for the
  **same** existing source ID; evidence alone never upgrades a disposition.

  Then, only if a measured count/diversity deficit remains, follow
  the separately authorized Section 9 source round. Do not execute source
  code. The round publication must add each immutable materialization receipt,
  its ledger/evidence-bundle generation, and acquisition-index entry before
  review or register publication. Reopen the actual acquired bytes offline,
  close the complete inventory, and audit rights, authorship, generation/edit
  lineage, privacy, polarity, family/pair identity, and every proposed record.
  Preassign two independent reviewers, seal their source/record decisions, and
  publish the blind receipt. Freeze the source-generation proposal only after
  those decisions, then create the separate proposal approval and immutable
  source generation. If review is unavailable/rejected or any inventory remains
  open, finish truthfully as `acquired_unreviewed`/`acquired_rejected`; do not
  create a source current pointer or register delta.

  Only after that post-download chain passes, publish exactly one generation-incrementing register delta for the
  round, containing its one or two genuinely new sources and every exact
  matching review; bind the round, each source receipt/materialization,
  parent/next register hashes, and prove no source/byte tree was already
  registered. `register:publish-round` alone owns each transaction-bound source
  staging directory, promotes each complete hash-named directory no-clobber,
  fsyncs every source `generations/` parent, and only then promotes source-
  current pointers and the register. The generation publishes all reviews and entries atomically. A missing review,
  unauthorized delta, or half-published generation leaves the prior register
  authoritative.

  For each accepted existing-source remediation or completed new-source round,
  run the exact full generation sequence before reading a deficit:
  source/evidence generations + record stream/overlap universe input -> bound
  overlap generation -> privacy/quality/lineage -> pre-witness/static generation
  -> `context:verify` brand -> smoke/canary search-result bundles -> transactional
  census/`require`. Use `rebuild:pre-witness` and the Task 5 Step 4 commands;
  never run census against stale authority. Then rerun the recursive gate block
  from Step 3.

### Task 8 — freeze an admission-complete 100/100 candidate set

**Files:**

- Modify external admission/census artifacts only.
- No-clobber publish the complete search authority at
  `/Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3/review/admission/witnesses/smoke/search-results/$SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256.json`
  and, after review, the complete review authority at

- [ ] **Step 1: generate the exact candidate witness without claiming readiness**

  Invoke `witness:search --gate smoke` and its distinct internal
  `witness:publish-search` action. Capture the returned exact hash-derived path
  and hash, then rebuild/replace the census from the verified pre-witness
  context with the exact smoke and canary search bundle plus publication-
  completion path/hash pairs. It must
  contain exactly 100 unique strict-gold witness units per polarity and a
  matching search receipt, but `ready=false` because no witness-review bundle
  exists yet. `require --gate smoke` must exit 1 and its only gate failure must
  be `witness_review_receipt_missing`; any count, diversity, context, search,
  or other failure returns to Tasks 5-7.

  ```bash
  SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    witness:search --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --gate smoke --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    witness:search --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --gate canary --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$CANARY_SEARCH_JSON")"
  ```

  Pass these eight exact bundle/completion path/hash values to candidate
  `census`; its resulting
  persisted census is the cross-step authority, not the shell variables.

- [ ] **Step 3: have the calibration reviewer inspect the exact 200 witness IDs**

  Verify polarity; the two-language minimum and per-language floor; the
  two-source, three-family, and 50%-cap gates; pair/cluster safety; license;
  edit status; and immutable resolution. This is still not a selection.

  Assign two reviewers before review, seal their decisions independently, then
  emit the post-decision blind receipt. Only afterward emit the schema-valid
  witness-review receipt binding the witness, both byte-identical independent
  regenerations and their receipts, constraint-check hash/receipt, and approved decisions. The witness
  itself contains none of those later IDs. Persist the exact gate-specific
  intents/tool receipts and complete witness-review bundle through:

  Store the Core-validated proposal at the content-addressed
  `review/admission/witnesses/smoke/proposals/$PROPOSAL_SHA256.json`, then
  capture the publisher result:

  ```bash
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- verify \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1 \
    --census review/eligible-census-v10.3.json
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultBundleRelativePath)' \
    /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3/review/eligible-census-v10.3.json)"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultBundleSha256)' \
    /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3/review/eligible-census-v10.3.json)"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultPublicationCompletionRelativePath)' \
    /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3/review/eligible-census-v10.3.json)"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultPublicationCompletionSha256)' \
    /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3/review/eligible-census-v10.3.json)"
  : "${PROPOSAL_SHA256:?set to the Core-validated proposal self-hash}"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_PROPOSAL="review/admission/witnesses/smoke/proposals/$PROPOSAL_SHA256.json"
  SMOKE_REVIEW_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- witness:publish-review \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --gate smoke \
    --bundle-proposal "$SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_PROPOSAL" \
    --search-bundle "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --search-bundle-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --search-publication-completion "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --search-publication-completion-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_REVIEW_JSON")"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_REVIEW_JSON")"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$SMOKE_REVIEW_JSON")"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$SMOKE_REVIEW_JSON")"
  ```

- [ ] **Step 4: rebuild the final census and require strict readiness**

  Replace the candidate census through Section 7 CAS, now binding the approved
  witness-review bundle's exact hash-derived relative path and SHA-256; no
  witness directory scan is permitted. Run `verify` twice, then require
  `require --gate smoke` exit 0. Construct and reverify the private
  `VerifiedReadyAdmissionCensusV1`; schema-valid bytes without that runtime
  proof are insufficient for Task 9B.

  ```bash
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- verify \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1 \
    --census review/eligible-census-v10.3.json
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- lint \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --all \
    --tool-profile admission-context-v1
  CENSUS_PATH=/Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3/review/eligible-census-v10.3.json
  REVIEW_REFERENCE_PATH=/Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3/review/admission/witnesses/smoke/projections/witness-review-reference.json
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultBundleRelativePath)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultBundleSha256)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultPublicationCompletionRelativePath)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.smoke.searchResultPublicationCompletionSha256)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.canary.searchResultBundleRelativePath)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.canary.searchResultBundleSha256)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.canary.searchResultPublicationCompletionRelativePath)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.canary.searchResultPublicationCompletionSha256)' \
    "$CENSUS_PATH")"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.bundleRelativePath)' \
    "$REVIEW_REFERENCE_PATH")"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.bundleSha256)' \
    "$REVIEW_REFERENCE_PATH")"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.publicationCompletionRelativePath)' \
    "$REVIEW_REFERENCE_PATH")"
  SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const fs=require("node:fs");const x=JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(process.argv[1],"utf8"));process.stdout.write(x.publicationCompletionSha256)' \
    "$REVIEW_REFERENCE_PATH")"
  CURRENT_SHA="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- \
    census:current-hash --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --census review/eligible-census-v10.3.json \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1)"
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- census \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --smoke-search-bundle "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-bundle-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$SMOKE_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --smoke-witness-review-bundle "$SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-witness-review-bundle-sha256 "$SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --smoke-witness-review-publication-completion "$SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --smoke-witness-review-publication-completion-sha256 "$SMOKE_WITNESS_REVIEW_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-bundle "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-bundle-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --canary-search-publication-completion-sha256 "$CANARY_SEARCH_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --tool-profile admission-census-v1 \
    --out review/eligible-census-v10.3.json \
    --replace-if-current-sha "$CURRENT_SHA"
  ```

- [ ] **Step 5: freeze census and input hashes**

  Re-run verify twice with no external change. Any difference reopens the
  affected source review.

- [ ] **Step 6: commit admission completion evidence**

  ```text
  docs(calibration): approve corpus admission for smoke
  ```

  Only after this commit may a separate authorized task create a corpus
  manifest from these admission records.

### Task 9A — bootstrap shared manifest dependency receipt contracts

**Scheduling:** This contract-only slice has no Task 8 or prerequisite-closure
dependency. Run it at a Core single-writer boundary before asking the release,
score/wire, run-lifecycle, or packed-runtime owners for their final receipts.
It creates no corpus manifest, changes no package version, and does not weaken
the Task 9B gate. After it lands, each upstream owner reruns its gate and emits
the matching schema-valid independently reviewed receipt.

**Files:**

- Create under `packages/core/schemas/v1/`:
  `calibration-release-prerequisite-approval.schema.json`,
  `calibration-score-wire-closure-receipt.schema.json`,
  `calibration-run-lifecycle-receipt.schema.json`, and
  `calibration-packed-runtime-receipt.schema.json`.
- Create: `packages/core/src/calibration-manifest-dependency-receipts.ts`
- Modify the Core schema index, codegen, exports, and validator harness; generate
  all four peers.
- Create:
  `packages/core/tests/calibration-manifest-dependency-receipts-contract.test.ts`
  plus valid, schema-invalid, semantic-invalid, and field-mutation fixtures.

- [x] **Step 1: write failing exact receipt-contract tests**

  Cover each version/kind, full 40-hex approved commit, plan/behavior/tarball/
  evidence hashes, exact Node 22/24 and package `0.45.0`, distinct sorted
  reviewers, terminal `approved`/exit-0 state, self-hash, unknown keys, and
  cross-kind/schema substitution. These independently reviewed receipts are
  terminal trust authorities over their subject commit/hash summaries; Task 9B
  reopens the receipt bytes but does not promise to discover or reopen unnamed
  internal test logs.

- [x] **Step 2: implement pure Core schemas, generated types, and validators**

  Add no I/O and no SlopBrick builder. Every JSON receipt has the exact schema
  `$id` used by the prerequisite referenced-artifact union in Task 9B.

- [x] **Step 3: run Core gates, review, and commit; recursive workspace gates remain downstream**

  ```bash
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core codegen
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core test:contract
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core validate:schema
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core typecheck
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core test
  corepack pnpm -r lint
  corepack pnpm -r typecheck
  corepack pnpm -r test
  corepack pnpm -r build
  git diff --check
  ```

  ```text
  feat(core): define calibration dependency receipts
  ```

### Task 9B — build the witness-bound Core corpus manifest

**Dependency:** Task 9A approved; Task 8 approved; release-asset plan Tasks 1-6
implemented and
independently approved for every witness source; score/wire validity closed;
and v10.3 run-init/post-scan verification implemented. Release-plan Tasks 7-8
are downstream, not prerequisites. The final `0.45.0` tarball's Node 22/24
proof is produced inside this task **after** the builder/version changes but
**before** any manifest output; it then joins the other evidence in the
schema-valid prerequisite bundle below. Final release/score/run and packed-
runtime receipts are intentionally emitted only after Task 9B's implementation
commit freezes the exact code they approve. Prose intent cannot start or skip a
gate in this task.

```ts
  readonly packedRuntimeReceiptSetSha256: string;
  readonly bindingSha256: string;
}

interface CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisiteBundleV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-manifest-prerequisites-v1';
  readonly bundleId: string;

  readonly manifestBuilder: {
    readonly behaviorSha256: string;

  };

    { readonly nodeMajor: 22; readonly tarballArtifactId: string; readonly receiptArtifactId: string },
    { readonly nodeMajor: 24; readonly tarballArtifactId: string; readonly receiptArtifactId: string },
  ];

  readonly referencedArtifactSetSha256: string;
  readonly bundleSha256: string;
}

type CalibrationAdmissionManifestReferencedArtifactV1 = {
  readonly artifactId: string;
  readonly relativePath: string;
  readonly bytes: number;
  readonly sha256: string;
} & (
  | {
      readonly kind: 'release_plan';
      readonly owner: 'release_asset_plan';
      readonly mediaType: 'text/markdown';
      readonly schemaId: null;
    }
  | {
      readonly kind: 'release_plan_approval';
      readonly owner: 'release_asset_plan';
      readonly mediaType: 'application/json';
      readonly schemaId: 'https://usebrick.dev/schemas/v1/calibration-release-prerequisite-approval.schema.json';
    }
  | {
      readonly kind: 'score_wire_closure_receipt';
      readonly owner: 'score_wire_gate';
      readonly mediaType: 'application/json';
      readonly schemaId: 'https://usebrick.dev/schemas/v1/calibration-score-wire-closure-receipt.schema.json';
    }
  | {
      readonly kind: 'run_init_receipt' | 'post_scan_receipt';
      readonly owner: 'run_lifecycle_gate';
      readonly mediaType: 'application/json';
      readonly schemaId: 'https://usebrick.dev/schemas/v1/calibration-run-lifecycle-receipt.schema.json';
    }
  | {
      readonly kind: 'packed_runtime_receipt';
      readonly owner: 'packed_runtime_matrix';
      readonly mediaType: 'application/json';
      readonly schemaId: 'https://usebrick.dev/schemas/v1/calibration-packed-runtime-receipt.schema.json';
    }
  | {
      readonly kind: 'package_tarball';
      readonly owner: 'packed_runtime_matrix';
      readonly mediaType: 'application/gzip';
      readonly schemaId: null;
    }
  | {
      readonly kind: 'manifest_builder';
      readonly owner: 'admission_manifest_builder';
      readonly mediaType: 'application/javascript';
      readonly schemaId: null;
      readonly packageTarballArtifactId: string;
      readonly packageMemberRelativePath: string;
    }
);

interface CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisiteStagingSetV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-manifest-prerequisite-staging-set-v1';
  readonly entries: readonly {
    readonly artifactId: string;
    readonly kind: CalibrationAdmissionManifestReferencedArtifactV1['kind'];
    readonly mediaType: CalibrationAdmissionManifestReferencedArtifactV1['mediaType'];
    readonly normalizedRelativePath: string;
    readonly bytes: number;
    readonly sha256: string;
  }[];
  readonly stagingSetSha256: string;
}

interface CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisitePublicationRequestV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-manifest-prerequisite-publication-request-v1';
  readonly requestId: string;
  readonly operation: 'create' | 'replace';
  readonly expectedCurrentState:
    | { readonly kind: 'absent' }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'existing';
        readonly bundleSha256: string;
        readonly currentSha256: string;
      };
  readonly sourceArtifacts: readonly (CalibrationAdmissionManifestReferencedArtifactV1 & {
    readonly source:
      | {
          readonly sourceRoot: 'platform_commit';
          readonly normalizedRelativePath: string;
          readonly approvedCommitSha: string;
        }
      | {
          readonly sourceRoot: 'prerequisite_staging';
          readonly normalizedRelativePath: string;
          readonly stagingSetSha256: string;
        };
  })[];
  readonly stagingSet: CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisiteStagingSetV1;
  readonly bundle: CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisiteBundleV1;
  readonly requestSha256: string;
}

interface CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisitePublicationTransactionV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-manifest-prerequisite-publication-transaction-v1';
  readonly transactionId: string;
  readonly lockSha256: string;
  readonly invocationIntentId: string;
  readonly requestId: string;
  readonly requestSha256: string;
  readonly operation: 'create' | 'replace';
  readonly expectedCurrentState:
    | { readonly kind: 'absent' }
    | {
        readonly kind: 'existing';
        readonly bundleSha256: string;
        readonly currentSha256: string;
      };
  readonly nextBundleSha256: string;
  readonly artifactSetSha256: string;
  readonly requestTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly requestFinalRelativePath: string;
  readonly artifacts: readonly {
    readonly artifactId: string;
    readonly stagedRelativePath: string;
    readonly finalRelativePath: string;
    readonly bytes: number;
    readonly sha256: string;
  }[];
  readonly bundleTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly bundleFinalRelativePath: string;
  readonly projectionTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly projectionFinalRelativePath:
    'review/admission/manifest-prerequisites/bundle.json';
  readonly completionTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly publicationCurrentTemporaryRelativePath: string;
  readonly publicationCurrentFinalRelativePath:
    'review/admission/manifest-prerequisites/publications/current.json';
  readonly recoveryNonce: string;
  readonly state:
    | {
        readonly phase:
          | 'intent_fsynced'
          | 'request_staged_fsynced'
          | 'request_promoted'
          | 'request_directory_fsynced'
          | 'artifacts_staged_fsynced'
          | 'artifacts_promoted'
          | 'artifact_directories_fsynced'
          | 'bundle_staged_fsynced'
          | 'bundle_promoted'
          | 'bundle_directory_fsynced'
          | 'projection_staged_fsynced'
          | 'projection_promoted'
          | 'projection_directory_fsynced';
      }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'publication_tool_receipt_started';
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase:
          | 'publication_tool_receipt_indexed'
          | 'completion_staged_fsynced'
          | 'completion_promoted'
          | 'completion_directory_fsynced'
          | 'publication_current_staged_fsynced'
          | 'publication_current_promoted'
          | 'publication_current_directory_fsynced'
          | 'complete';
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
        readonly publicationToolReceiptId: string;
        readonly publicationToolReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
        readonly completionSha256: string;
        readonly completionFinalRelativePath: string;
        readonly publicationCurrentSha256: string;
      };
  readonly transactionSha256: string;
}
```
