```ts
  readonly currentSha256: string;
  readonly generationRelativePath: string;
  readonly generationSha256: string;
  readonly buildReceiptRelativePath: string;
  readonly buildReceiptSha256: string;
  readonly manifestRelativePath: string;
  readonly manifestSha256: string;
  readonly referenceSha256: string;
}

interface CalibrationAdmissionManifestPublicationLockV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-manifest-publication-lock-v1';
  readonly lockId: string;
  readonly intendedTransactionId: string;
  readonly invocationIntentId: string;
  readonly manifestId: 'v10.3-admission-smoke' | 'v10.3-admission-canary';
  readonly operation: 'create' | 'replace';
  readonly expectedCurrentState:
    | { readonly kind: 'absent' }
    | { readonly kind: 'existing'; readonly generationSha256: string };
  readonly manifestSha256: string;
  readonly prerequisiteBundleSha256: string;
  readonly recoveryNonce: string;
  readonly lockSha256: string;
}

interface CalibrationAdmissionManifestPublicationTransactionV1 {
  readonly version: 'v10.3-admission-manifest-publication-transaction-v1';
  readonly transactionId: string;
  readonly lockSha256: string;
  readonly invocationIntentId: string;
  readonly manifestId: 'v10.3-admission-smoke' | 'v10.3-admission-canary';
  readonly operation: 'create' | 'replace';
  readonly expectedCurrentState:
    | { readonly kind: 'absent' }
    | { readonly kind: 'existing'; readonly generationSha256: string };
  readonly manifestSha256: string;
  readonly prerequisiteBundleSha256: string;
  readonly manifestStagingRelativePath: string;
  readonly buildReceiptStagingRelativePath: string;
  readonly generationLeafNames: readonly ['manifest.json', 'build-receipt.json', 'generation.json'];
  readonly recoveryNonce: string;
  readonly state:
    | { readonly phase: 'intent_fsynced' | 'manifest_staged_fsynced' }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'tool_receipt_publication_started';
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase: 'tool_receipt_indexed';
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
        readonly toolReceiptId: string;
        readonly toolReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
      }
    | {
        readonly phase:
          | 'build_receipt_staged_fsynced'
          | 'generation_directory_staged_fsynced'
          | 'generation_directory_promoted'
          | 'generations_parent_fsynced'
          | 'current_temporary_fsynced'
          | 'current_promoted'
          | 'output_directories_fsynced'
          | 'complete';
        readonly toolReceiptId: string;
        readonly toolReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly toolAuthorityIndexSha256: string;
        readonly nestedHandoffSha256: string;
        readonly childTransactionId: string;
        readonly childRecoveryNonce: string;
        readonly buildReceiptId: string;
        readonly buildReceiptSha256: string;
        readonly generationSha256: string;
        readonly generationDirectoryStagedRelativePath: string;
        readonly generationDirectoryFinalRelativePath: string;
        readonly currentTemporaryRelativePath: string;
        readonly currentFinalRelativePath: string;
      };
  readonly transactionSha256: string;
}

declare const verifiedManifestPrerequisitesBrand: unique symbol;
type VerifiedAdmissionManifestPrerequisitesV1 = Readonly<{
  readonly bundle: CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisiteBundleV1;
  readonly publicationRequest: CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisitePublicationRequestV1;
  readonly publicationCompletion: CalibrationAdmissionManifestPrerequisitePublicationCompletionV1;
  readonly [verifiedManifestPrerequisitesBrand]: true;
}>;

declare function verifyAdmissionManifestPrerequisites(
  root: string,
  input: unknown,
): Promise<
  | { readonly ok: true; readonly value: VerifiedAdmissionManifestPrerequisitesV1 }
  | { readonly ok: false; readonly errors: readonly string[] }
>;

declare function buildCorpusManifestFromAdmission(input: {
  ready: VerifiedReadyAdmissionCensusV1;
  prerequisites: VerifiedAdmissionManifestPrerequisitesV1;
}): SlopbrickCalibrationCorpusManifestV103;
```

The prerequisite symbol is not sufficient authority. Its SlopBrick module
also owns a private `WeakSet`; the verifier reopens and hashes every referenced
artifact/approval/tarball, deep-freezes the exact verified object, and registers
only that identity. The builder checks WeakSet membership before deriving any
output, so casts, clones, deserialization, cross-module objects, or altered
bytes fail before manifest creation.

Every prerequisite byte is content-addressed beneath
`review/admission/manifest-prerequisites/`: JSON/Markdown artifacts use
`artifacts/$KIND/$SHA256`, including the JavaScript builder artifact under
`artifacts/manifest_builder/$SHA256`; package bytes use
`tarballs/$SHA256.tgz`, and every prerequisite bundle uses
`bundles/$BUNDLE_SHA256.json`. The fixed `bundle.json` is only a byte-equal
current projection. `relativePath` is
normalized and must equal the path derived from `kind` and `sha256`; the
kind/owner/media-type/schema mapping is closed and semantic validation rejects
an absent schema for a JSON receipt, an unexpected schema, duplicate artifact
ID/hash/path, an unreferenced artifact, or a reference outside this root. The
release-plan approval receipt owns and validates its approved commit/plan hash;
the score-wire receipt owns its commit; the two run-lifecycle receipts own
their commit; each packed-runtime receipt owns its Node major and the same
tarball artifact and must use that same `approvedCommitSha`. All release,
score, run-lifecycle, and packed-runtime receipt commits must equal the Task 9B
implementation commit recorded by the prerequisite bundle. The verifier performs no platform-worktree or directory
discovery and needs no second authority root.

`manifest:publish-prerequisites` is the only writer for this tree. It runs
offline under `admission-manifest-v1` from one Core-validated publication
request whose sources contain no absolute path. `release_plan` must use
`sourceRoot=platform_commit`, a normalized relative path, and the exact
approved 40-hex implementation commit; the publisher verifies the Git object
at that commit without trusting mutable worktree bytes. Approval/closure/run/
runtime receipts, `package_tarball`, and `manifest_builder` must use
`sourceRoot=prerequisite_staging`, a normalized relative path, and the exact
closed staging-set hash. The builder JavaScript is the exact no-follow regular
file member extracted from the content-addressed package tarball; its recorded
member path, bytes, and SHA must match the same member when the tarball is
reopened. The two actual root paths are explicit CLI inputs but normalize in
the invocation intent to `@platform-commit` and `@prerequisite-staging`; actual
host paths remain local diagnostics. Both are realpath/no-follow contained and
may not be crossed by kind. Before prerequisite-tree mutation it rehashes every source against the request, derives all
final paths from kind/hash, persists and indexes the invocation intent through
the recursion-breaking tool-authority publisher, then creates/fsyncs
the fixed lock (including `intendedTransactionId`) and transaction. It first
writes/fsyncs/no-clobber promotes the complete request itself to
`requests/$REQUEST_SHA256.json`, then writes
transaction-bound `wx` temporaries, fsyncs, no-clobber promotes every artifact,
fsyncs their parents, computes and no-clobber publishes the immutable bundle,
and promotes the fixed projection last by exact expected-current CAS. It then
indexes an external post-output publication tool receipt through the nested
tool-authority handoff and publishes the hash-derived completion object at
`publications/completions/$COMPLETION_SHA256.json`. The bundle deliberately
omits that future receipt/completion; the completion binds both without a hash
cycle and stores the immutable request path/hash so post-cleanup verification
can re-open the complete source-root/commit/staging proof. It embeds the exact
completed publication-tool handoff and requires byte equality with its
immutable twin before transient cleanup. Finally it CAS-
promotes `publications/current.json`, whose self-hashed
bytes bind the exact immutable bundle and completion paths/hashes. That current
reference—not a bundle-derived completion filename—is the durable routing root.
Post-cleanup verification resolves the completion's publication receipt and
invocation intent, requires the intent input set to bind the exact request SHA,
recomputes the named request/artifact-set/bundle primary-output projection, and
requires equality with both `namedPrimaryOutputProjectionSha256` and the tool
receipt's `outputSetSha256`.

The embedded staging set is not an asserted digest. Its entries are sorted and
unique by `{normalizedRelativePath,artifactId}` and contain exact
`{artifactId,kind,mediaType,normalizedRelativePath,bytes,sha256}` tuples;
`stagingSetSha256` is the canonical SHA-256 of that array with no omitted
fields. The publisher no-follow reopens every tuple beneath
`@prerequisite-staging`, recomputes byte/hash/media semantics, and requires the
tuple set to equal exactly all and only request artifacts whose
`sourceRoot=prerequisite_staging`. Omitted, extra, reordered, duplicate, or
substituted staging members fail before the lock.
`sourceArtifacts` is sorted/unique by `artifactId` and is set-equal to the
bundle's `referencedArtifacts`; every shared kind/owner/media/schema/path/bytes/
hash field must be identical, with `source` as the only request-only member.
Thus a request cannot publish an unbundled byte or omit a bundled prerequisite.

If the exact bundle/request/artifact set is already current,
`manifest:publish-prerequisites` reopens the existing completion and returns
the same reference without creating a transaction or tool receipt. This is the
sole completed-request replay exception: it does not reinterpret the original
create/replace expected state, because the current completion proves that exact
request already committed. The same
current bundle with a different request is rejected as an ambiguous replay.
After switching to another bundle, switching back may create a new completion
keyed by its own hash and advances the current reference by exact CAS; it never
collides with or overwrites the earlier completion.

`manifest:recover-prerequisites (--transaction-id <id> | --from-lock)` requires
the recovery nonce and no-live-writer acknowledgement, validates every staged/
final byte plus expected/current projection, and rolls forward or restores the
exact prior projection without removing unknown paths. It handles lock-only
crashes, removes/fsyncs transaction before lock, and is idempotent at every
write/rename/fsync/tool-index/unlink boundary. Every manifest build receipt
records the immutable bundle, publication completion, and publication request
paths/hashes, never `bundle.json` or `publications/current.json`. Historical
`manifest:verify` starts only from those receipt-pinned immutable references,
so every prior manifest generation remains re-openable after later prerequisite
replacement or a switch-away/switch-back.
`manifest:verify-prerequisites` is strictly read-only: it accepts the current
bundle projection only as routing input, requires it to match
`publications/current.json`, then requires the exact immutable twin and matching
hash-addressed publication completion/tool receipt. It reopens all referenced bytes and prints
canonical `{relativePath,sha256,completionRelativePath,completionSha256,
requestRelativePath,requestSha256}` for the immutable graph. It also accepts
that complete six-field immutable graph directly for historical/canary reuse;
partial refs or a mix with mutable current are invalid.

The canonical builder artifact SHA is the defined builder behavior hash. It
must equal `manifestBuilder.behaviorSha256`, the manifest-build invocation
intent/tool receipt `executableBehaviorSha256`, both packed-runtime receipts'
`manifestBuilderBehaviorSha256`, the manifest `admissionBinding` behavior hash,
and the build receipt behavior hash. Any inequality invalidates prerequisites
before publication. Tests reopen the package tarball, locate the one canonical
builder member by its frozen package-relative path, and require byte/hash
equality with the staged `manifest_builder`; an untracked worktree `dist/` file,
second matching member, path substitution, or post-pack rebuild fails.

Add optional nullable schema field `admissionBinding` with JSON Schema
`default: null`; when present and non-null it has the exact
`CalibrationAdmissionManifestBindingV1` shape plus per-file
`admissionRecordId` and `materializationId`. The new admission-backed method is
exactly `methodVersion = v10.3.2` and semantically requires all of them.
Omitted and explicit `null` both mean `legacy_non_admission` to the pure
semantic validator, but canonicalization does not insert the default, so old
manifest bytes/IDs remain stable. That legacy state is valid only for the
already-defined `v10.3.0`/`v10.3.1` methods and can never satisfy the admission
builder, admission verifier, or an admission manifest-ID consumer; conversely,
`v10.3.2` rejects omitted/null binding before output or mutation. A non-null
binding on a legacy method is also invalid. `verifiedContextSha256`,
`eligibilitySnapshotSha256`, `censusSha256`, `admissionRecordsSha256`,
`sourceReviewSetSha256`, `evidenceIndexSha256`, `evidencePayloadSetSha256`,
`evidenceReceiptSetSha256`, `toolProfileSetSha256`, `toolReceiptSetSha256`,
`blindReviewReceiptSetSha256`, `temporalAttestationSetSha256`, and
`materializationReceiptSetSha256` must equal the private ready census/context.
`witnessSha256`, `searchResultBundleSha256`,
`searchResultPublicationCompletionSha256`, `witnessReviewBundleSha256`,
`witnessReviewPublicationCompletionSha256`, and the canonical sorted receipt-
set hash across that review bundle's search,
regeneration, constraint-check, blind-review, and witness-review receipts must
equal the exact gate bundle pinned by the census.
`prerequisiteBundleSha256`, `manifestBuilderBehaviorSha256`, and the canonical
sorted Node-22/24 `packedRuntimeReceiptSetSha256` must equal the verified
prerequisite bundle. `bindingSha256` self-hashes exactly these fields with only
itself omitted. Existing older manifests remain schema-valid and byte-stable,
but the admission builder/verifier rejects `v10.3.2` when any field/equality is
absent. The post-output manifest tool/build receipts are intentionally **not**
inside `admissionBinding`; the immutable generation binds their exact hashes,
avoiding a manifest/receipt fixed point.

The manifest never embeds its future build/publication receipt. Publication is
strictly one-way: verified ready census + verified prerequisite bundle ->
canonical manifest -> post-output manifest tool receipt -> build receipt ->
immutable manifest generation -> self-hashed current pointer. The build receipt
binds the manifest, prerequisite bundle, builder behavior, packed-runtime
receipt set, exact ready census/witness, intent/tool receipt, transaction, and
prior-current CAS. It embeds the completed manifest-tool handoff and revalidates
its immutable twin before the transient handoff is removed. The generation binds that receipt; the current pointer binds
the generation. `manifest:verify` begins from the named manifest current
pointer, resolves generation/build receipt/manifest/prerequisites by exact
contained paths, reconstructs both private brands, and rejects a flat manifest
projection, orphan generation, or missing/mismatched receipt.
On success, `manifest:verify --manifest-id ...` prints one compact canonical
`CalibrationAdmissionManifestReferenceV1`. Every path is normalized,
corpus-root-relative, and contained; every SHA is lowercase. The self-hashed
`referenceSha256` is the canonical SHA-256 of the complete object with only
`referenceSha256` omitted. The reference pins the exact current pointer bytes, immutable generation, build
receipt, and manifest leaf. It is routing input only, never authority. Each
downstream process must reopen that named current pointer, require its bytes to
still match `currentSha256`, follow and recheck the exact immutable generation,
build receipt, manifest, and prerequisite graph, reconstruct the private
authority in that same process, and reread the current pointer immediately
before its first output or mutation. A current advance fails even when it
reuses the same manifest leaf bytes.

- [ ] **Step 1: write failing round-trip and no-invention tests**

  Cover Git and every release-archive field, `materializationId`, repository
  mapping, `archiveFormat`, `rootPrefix`, per-asset rights, path relativity,
  missing/wrong roots, extra folder files, witness mutation, sensitivity/
  quarantine injection, and unapproved dependency state. Mutate every
  prerequisite commit/artifact/receipt/tarball hash, use a schema-valid but
  unverified census instead of the private ready brand, and substitute the
  other gate's witness bundle. A cast/clone/deserialized prerequisite bundle
  must also fail its private brand. Mutate every referenced-artifact
  kind/owner/path/media/schema/bytes/hash mapping and require failure without
  platform-worktree discovery. All must fail before output creation.
  Preserve byte-identical legacy `v10.3.0`/`v10.3.1` fixtures with omitted and
  explicit-null `admissionBinding` (`default: null`), reject a non-null binding
  on either legacy method, and reject both omitted/null binding for exact
  admission method `v10.3.2`. Prove the admission builder/verifier and manifest-
  ID consumers never accept the legacy default as admission authority.
  For each of `corpus:validate`, `materialize`, and `select`, prove exact
  `v10.3.2` rejects flat `--manifest` input even when its expected leaf hash is
  correct; requires one complete canonical `--manifest-ref-json` together with
  matching `--root`, `--manifest-id`, and
  `--expected-manifest-sha256`; and rejects mixed or partial legacy/admission
  arguments. Independently mutate the reference, current pointer, generation,
  build receipt, manifest, and prerequisite graph and require each CLI to fail
  before success output, cache/output creation, or selection writes. Advance
  current to a different valid generation that reuses the same manifest leaf,
  and inject an advance between initial verification and the pre-output reread;
  both must fail. Preserve the release Task 6 legacy flat-path behavior for
  only `v10.3.0`/`v10.3.1`.

  Extend the clean packed-consumer fixture in this task, not later release
  documentation. Install the exact Task 9B package tarball into a new project
  with no workspace-source resolution, construct one tiny fully valid
  current -> generation -> build-receipt -> v10.3.2 manifest -> prerequisite
  graph, and run the packed `corpus:validate`, `materialize`, and `select`
  commands through the complete admission reference. Assert all three succeed
  offline, their portable outputs are deterministic/path-free, and every graph
  mutation/current advance above fails before output. Run the unchanged legacy
  v10.3.0/v10.3.1 packed fixtures in the same suite so admission support cannot
  silently remove compatibility.

  Prerequisite-publication tests cover both source-root union branches,
  normalized-relative-path containment/no-follow, platform commit/staging-set
  hash binding, every forbidden kind/root crossing, kind/hash-derived
  destinations, create/replace CAS, same-byte idempotence,
  occupied different-byte collision, fixed-projection-last ordering, external
  publication receipt/completion binding, and a read-only verifier that cannot
  write. Require exact-current same-bundle/same-request reuse with no new
  transaction/receipt, reject same-current-bundle/new-request replay, and cover
  switch-away/switch-back with two distinct content-addressed completions and
  exact current-reference CAS. Kill throughout pre-output invocation-intent
  tool-index publication, then at lock-file/lock-directory fsync before transaction creation and
  every later artifact/bundle/projection/tool-receipt/completion write, rename,
  fsync, and unlink. `--from-lock` must recover with no unwritten transaction ID,
  retain prior immutable bundles, restore the exact prior projection when
  rollback is required, and remove no unknown path.
  Reorder, omit, add, duplicate, or substitute a staging tuple/file and require
  exact staging/request-set rejection; after cleanup, substitute/delete the
  immutable request or its completion path/hash and require read-only verifier
  failure. Mutate completion intent ID or named output projection, receipt
  input/output hashes, or request/artifact/bundle projection membership and
  require failure.

  Publication tests kill before/after every manifest/tool-receipt/build-receipt/
  generation/current-pointer write, rename, unlink, and file/directory fsync.
  They also kill after manifest lock-file/lock-directory fsync before transaction
  creation and recover through `manifest:recover --from-lock` with no unwritten
  transaction ID.
  Cover first create, exact-hash replace, stale current, two writers, same-byte
  idempotence, changed-byte collision, prior-generation restore, orphan flat
  projection, transaction-before-lock cleanup, and recovery that removes no
  unknown path. Replace prerequisite current after publishing two manifest
  generations, then reverify each prior manifest solely through its build-
  receipt-pinned immutable bundle/completion/request paths; mutable prerequisite
  current or directory discovery must not participate. Graph tests prove manifest -> tool receipt -> build receipt ->
  generation -> current with no future receipt embedded in manifest bytes.

- [ ] **Step 2: implement the prerequisite verifier and pure conversion**

  Implement without creating an external manifest.
  `manifest:verify-prerequisites` reopens every schema-valid approval/receipt,
  checks exact approved commits and referenced artifact bytes, and proves both
  Node receipts bind the same content-addressed package-tarball artifact. It
  resolves only the bundle's typed contained paths and closed kind/owner/schema
  mapping. The pure builder then reads only
  the private ready context/census/witness bundle and its internally bound
  admission records. Map one archive asset to one exact manifest repository;
  never default/invent a field or discover directory members. Validate with
  Core before returning.

  The standalone verifier is audit-only because a private WeakSet brand cannot
  cross a process boundary. `manifest:build` must reopen/reverify the
  exact immutable prerequisite bundle/completion/request triple passed with
  expected hashes, plus the pre-witness context, census, and witness-review bundle, and
  construct both private brands inside its own process immediately before it
  calls the pure builder.

  Task 9B also completes the consumer integration that release Task 6 could
  only reserve before this verifier existed. Add one shared
  `openAdmissionManifestForConsumer` boundary in
  `admission-manifest-consumer.ts`. Its input is exactly
  `{root, manifestId, manifestReference, expectedManifestSha256}`; it parses a
  canonical `CalibrationAdmissionManifestReferenceV1`, reopens and validates
  the whole current -> generation -> build-receipt -> manifest -> prerequisite
  graph, compares the independent expected leaf SHA, deep-freezes the resolved
  manifest/reference, and registers that exact object identity in a module-
  private `WeakSet`. It then rereads and rehashes current before returning a
  branded value. No serialized reference, cast, clone, prior
  `manifest:verify` stdout, or leaf path/hash pair can create the brand.

  In `scripts/cal/v103.ts`, the `corpus:validate`, `materialize`, and `select`
  admission mode requires all four CLI inputs
  `--root`, `--manifest-id`, `--manifest-ref-json`, and
  `--expected-manifest-sha256`; each command calls the shared boundary inside
  its own process and passes the still-branded object directly to its operation.
  The operation checks WeakSet membership and performs one final current-pointer
  reread before emitting success or creating/mutating any cache, checkout map,
  run directory, selection JSONL, or ledger. Admission mode rejects
  `--manifest`. The mutually exclusive legacy mode remains
  `--manifest + --expected-manifest-sha256` and accepts only methods
  `v10.3.0`/`v10.3.1`; it cannot parse or downgrade `v10.3.2`. Ambiguous,
  partial, or cross-mode arguments exit 2. Task 9B owns these changes before
  its implementation commit, package tarball, Node 22/24 receipts, and
  prerequisite approval freeze; release Tasks 7-8 may only consume/reverify
  them, never add the integration later.

- [ ] **Step 3: freeze release metadata and prove the final packed runtimes**

  Apply the single `0.44.0` -> `0.45.0` bump, add the top CHANGELOG entry and
  exact docs. Tests assert package version, top CHANGELOG header, documented
  CLI, manifest method version, private Core `0.3.0`, SlopBrick's exact
  `workspace:^0.3.0` range, lockfile, and bundled generated contracts agree.
  Run the complete Step 5 Core schema/
  codegen/type/test, SlopBrick lint/type/full-test/build, recursive gate, and
  `git diff --check` matrix, then make the explicit implementation commit:

  ```text
  feat(calibration): build admission-bound corpus manifests
  ```

  Record:

  ```bash
  BUILDER_COMMIT_SHA="$(git rev-parse HEAD)"
  ```

  From that exact commit,
  rerun and independently approve release-materialization Task 6, score/wire
  closure, run-init, and post-scan gates; the Task 6 rerun must include the
  clean-tarball v10.3.2 validate/materialize/select flow above. Emit their Task 9A-schema receipts
  with `approvedCommitSha = BUILDER_COMMIT_SHA`. Build one package tarball from
  the same commit and run that same hash in clean Node 22 and 24 consumers,
  emitting both packed-runtime receipts. Content-address the plan, receipts,
  builder artifact extracted from that tarball, and tarball through the sole
  prerequisite publisher; it assembles the immutable bundle and completion:

  ```bash
  : "${PREREQUISITE_PUBLICATION_REQUEST:?set to the reviewed Core-valid request}"
  : "${PREREQUISITE_STAGING_ROOT:?set to the closed receipt/tarball staging root}"
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- manifest:publish-prerequisites \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --request "$PREREQUISITE_PUBLICATION_REQUEST" \
    --platform-root /Users/cheng/platform \
    --prerequisite-staging-root "$PREREQUISITE_STAGING_ROOT" \
    --operation create \
    --expect-current-absent \
    --tool-profile admission-manifest-v1
  ```

  The request is frozen before its invocation intent; the intent's input set
  binds `requestSha256`, while the request contains no future intent ID.
  Do not carry publisher stdout through task boundaries. Step 4 re-resolves the
  durable `publications/current.json` -> immutable completion -> immutable
  request/bundle graph through the read-only verifier.

  No package, schema, builder, test, or product-doc byte may change after the
  implementation commit. Such a change invalidates every commit-bound receipt
  and both runtime receipts, requiring a new implementation commit, rerun, and
  rebuilt prerequisite bundle. The later Task 9B evidence commit may change
  only the platform admission evidence document, which is explicitly outside
  package/tarball/builder inputs.

  Before writing any external manifest, rerun the packed-consumer checks and
  verify the scoped implementation paths are byte-identical to
  `BUILDER_COMMIT_SHA`. Only that green, clean, receipt-complete state may
  proceed to Step 4.

- [ ] **Step 4: create, verify, and round-trip the manifest operatively**

  ```bash
  PREREQUISITE_REF_JSON="$(corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- manifest:verify-prerequisites \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --prerequisites review/admission/manifest-prerequisites/bundle.json \
    --tool-profile admission-context-v1)"
  PREREQUISITE_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.relativePath)' \
    "$PREREQUISITE_REF_JSON")"
  PREREQUISITE_BUNDLE_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.sha256)' \
    "$PREREQUISITE_REF_JSON")"
  PREREQUISITE_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionRelativePath)' \
    "$PREREQUISITE_REF_JSON")"
  PREREQUISITE_COMPLETION_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.completionSha256)' \
    "$PREREQUISITE_REF_JSON")"
  PREREQUISITE_REQUEST_RELATIVE_PATH="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.requestRelativePath)' \
    "$PREREQUISITE_REF_JSON")"
  PREREQUISITE_REQUEST_SHA256="$(node -e \
    'const x=JSON.parse(process.argv[1]);process.stdout.write(x.requestSha256)' \
    "$PREREQUISITE_REF_JSON")"
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- manifest:build \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --manifest-id v10.3-admission-smoke \
    --census review/eligible-census-v10.3.json \
    --prerequisites "$PREREQUISITE_BUNDLE_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --expected-prerequisites-sha256 "$PREREQUISITE_BUNDLE_SHA256" \
    --prerequisite-publication-completion "$PREREQUISITE_COMPLETION_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --expected-prerequisite-publication-completion-sha256 "$PREREQUISITE_COMPLETION_SHA256" \
    --prerequisite-publication-request "$PREREQUISITE_REQUEST_RELATIVE_PATH" \
    --expected-prerequisite-publication-request-sha256 "$PREREQUISITE_REQUEST_SHA256" \
    --operation create \
    --expect-current-absent \
    --tool-profile admission-manifest-v1 \
    --manifest-root manifests/v10.3-admission-smoke
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- manifest:verify \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --manifest-id v10.3-admission-smoke \
    --tool-profile admission-context-v1
  ```

  `manifest:build` derives the exact smoke witness-review relative path and hash
  from the reverified ready census and reopens that hash-addressed bundle. It
  also reopens and rehashes the immutable prerequisite path captured from the
  verifier and requires exact equality with
  `--expected-prerequisites-sha256`, then reopens the captured publication
  completion and request under their own expected hashes. It never rereads
  `bundle.json` or `publications/current.json`. A mutable
  projection replacement between verification and build therefore cannot
  switch approved inputs. It accepts no shell variable or alternate witness
  path across the Task 8 commit boundary.

  Build is no-clobber by default; replacement uses `--operation replace` and
  requires the exact current generation SHA. It refuses any output outside the
  manifest-ID-specific contained root and promotes `current.json` last. Only after
  `manifest:verify` succeeds does the
  following round trip run:

  `source review + admission record -> Core manifest -> checkout map ->
  resolver -> exact bytes` must succeed offline for Git and release assets and
  fail on any root/materialization/receipt mismatch.

  On interruption, do not rerun build. After confirming no live writer, invoke
  recovery separately, then run `manifest:verify` only if recovery reports a
  completed generation:

  ```bash
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run cal:admission -- manifest:recover \
    --root /Users/cheng/corpus-expansion/v10.3 \
    --manifest-id v10.3-admission-smoke \
    --from-lock \
    --recovery-nonce "$MANIFEST_PUBLICATION_RECOVERY_NONCE" \
    --tool-profile admission-manifest-v1 \
    --acknowledge-no-live-writer
  ```

  Recovery is not part of the clean success block; without a journal it exits
  2 with `no_recovery_required` and changes nothing.

- [ ] **Step 5: run full gates and commit evidence only**

  Rerun the entire Step 3 pre-output matrix after external manifest
  verification and byte round-trip evidence. Both runs must be green.
  Before committing, verify every Task 9B implementation/package/schema/test/doc
  path is byte-identical to `BUILDER_COMMIT_SHA`. Stage only
  `packages/slopbrick/docs/calibration/v10.3-corpus-source-admission-evidence.md`;
  changing any package input reopens Step 3 and all approvals.

  ```bash
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core codegen
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core test:contract
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core validate:schema
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core typecheck
  corepack pnpm --filter @usebrick/core test
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick exec vitest run \
    tests/calibration/v103-admission-manifest.test.ts \
    tests/calibration/v103-admission-manifest-publication.test.ts \
    tests/calibration/v103-admission-manifest-consumer.test.ts \
    tests/calibration/v103-cli-e2e.test.ts \
    tests/calibration/v103-materialize-sources.test.ts \
    tests/integration/pack-consumer.test.ts
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick lint
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick typecheck
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick test
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick build
  corepack pnpm --filter slopbrick run test:pack-matrix -- --node 22 --node 24
  corepack pnpm -r lint
  corepack pnpm -r typecheck
  corepack pnpm -r test
  corepack pnpm -r build
  git diff --check
  ```

  ```text
  docs(calibration): record admission manifest proof
  ```

### Task 10 — execute the manifest-derived 100/100 smoke

**Dependency:** Task 9B round trip approved.

- [ ] Verify the manifest, exact witness/selection identity, checkout/
  materialization map, and all hashes before scanning. Folder discovery is
  forbidden.
- [ ] Execute two smoke runs, including controlled zero-fire/timeout/failure/
  resume cases, and enforce Section 8.1. No threshold or registry change occurs
  in the same commit.
- [ ] Obtain independent corpus and calibration review; reject claims broader
  than represented languages/sources.
- [ ] Commit smoke evidence only:

  ```text
  test(calibration): record v10.3 admission smoke
  ```

### Task 11 — expand, census, and freeze the exact 10k canary

**Dependency:** Task 10 passes twice.

- [ ] **Step 1: rerun census against all newly reviewed admission records**

  Require 5,000/5,000 strict gold, at least ten source checkouts per polarity,
  complete source-cap capacity accounting, and every Section 8.2 diversity
  cap. Marginal success sets only `countReady`.

- [ ] **Step 2: use bounded acquisition rounds only for measured deficits**

  Stop after every separately authorized maximum-two-source round to regenerate
  and independently review the census. Never imply one round can provide the
  derived ten-source minimum.

- [ ] **Step 3: freeze exact 10,000 IDs and method policy**

  Generate the exact 10,000-unit witness, search receipt, and search-result
  bundle with gate-specific intents/receipts and
  `canary.ready=false`; `require --gate canary` must exit 1 solely for the
  missing witness review. Independently regenerate identical witness bytes
  twice under two distinct persisted intents/receipts and run a separately
  receipted constraint check. Preassign two calibration reviewers, seal their witness decisions,
  emit the post-decision blind receipt and witness-review receipt, and persist
  the complete gate-specific search and review authorities through
  `witness:search`/`witness:publish-search` at
  `witnesses/canary/search-results/$SEARCH_BUNDLE_SHA256.json` and
  `witness:publish-review` at
  `witnesses/canary/witness-reviews/$REVIEW_BUNDLE_SHA256.json`, including all
  invocation intents/tool receipts. Capture each publisher's canonical bundle
  and publication-completion path/hash JSON exactly as in Task 8; a proven or indeterminate
  certificate leaves `canary.ready=false`. The seed, solver, source/family
  caps, language quotas, hashes, scanner package, registry, signal table, and
  admission policy are immutable inputs.

- [ ] **Step 4: replace/reverify the census and require canary readiness**

  Rebuild through census CAS with exact canary search/review bundle and
  publication-completion relative paths/hashes plus the unchanged smoke bundle/
  completion references, run `verify` twice, require `require --gate canary`
  exit 0, and construct the private
  `VerifiedReadyAdmissionCensusV1` for the canary gate.

- [ ] **Step 5: build and verify the canary admission manifest**

  Reuse Task 9B's approved six-field immutable prerequisite graph (bundle,
  publication completion, and request paths/hashes)—never mutable prerequisite
  current—and the manifest builder with the
  canary `VerifiedReadyAdmissionCensusV1`. Invoke `manifest:build` with
  `--manifest-id v10.3-admission-canary --operation create
  --expect-current-absent` plus all six Task 9B prerequisite path/hash flags;
  it derives and revalidates the exact canary review
  bundle from the ready census and publishes beneath the manifest-ID generation
  root. Verify through `manifest:verify --manifest-id
  v10.3-admission-canary`, then verify the complete offline
  source-review/record/manifest/resolver byte round trip, and prove the manifest
  contains exactly the 10,000 witness IDs before creating selection or run
  state.

- [ ] **Step 6: run the two-run canary and enforce Section 8.2**

  A coverage, parity, privacy, overlap, or determinism failure makes it
  diagnostic-only.

- [ ] **Step 7: independent method-freeze review and commit**

  ```text
  test(calibration): freeze v10.3 canary method
  ```

## 12. Verification matrix

| Requirement | Positive test | Mandatory failure/mutation |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Offline proof-carrying context | every claim resolves through index -> CAS payload -> actual bytes -> evidence/tool receipt | arbitrary hash, deleted/substituted CAS object, stale/replayed receipt, network fallback |
| Runtime authority ownership | Core durable validators pass, then SlopBrick factory returns registered frozen context | cast/clone/deserialization, Core disposition call, context from another module instance |
| Policy/tool receipts | every action uses its exact schema-valid task profile and receipt | broad bootstrap prose, cross-profile replay, undeclared executable/network/resource |
| Nested publication recovery | profiled child intent-authority companion completes before output child; every parent fsyncs branch-correct transient handoffs, every lock stores the intended transaction ID, and witness/prerequisite/manifest completions additionally re-open their embedded immutable twins | missing/extra companion, child mutation before intent index, fabricated infrastructure intent/receipt, missing/substituted required twin, lock-only crash without `--from-lock`, child discovery |
| Immutable generation paths | generation-local leaf receipts resolve through an exact self-hashed current pointer; source/overlap generations use whole-directory no-clobber promotion/parent fsync; independently addressed CAS uses hash-derived root paths | outer generation hash in leaf receipt, flat projection authority, partial directory set accepted, prior generation unreadable after replacement |
| Source-review completeness | initial register/review sets equal 329; every later current set remains exactly equal after an acquisition-bound delta | omitted/extra/template review, existing-leaf promotion changes count, unauthorized new entry |
| Blind review | assignment -> two decisions -> post-decision receipt, with acyclic IDs | peer/receipt ID in decision, pre-seal peer visibility, missing/mismatched receipt |
| Eligible census | 0/0 valid; witnessed 100/100 and 5k/5k ready | marginal-only or directory count presented as readiness |
| Exact witness/review | result -> search receipt -> blind review -> witness review -> census | cyclic receipt ID, all marginals pass but no feasible cohort, mutated/unreviewed witness |
| Witness publication | computation receipt exists before bundle; distinct no-clobber search/review publisher receipt is bound by a hash-addressed completion; census pins exact bundle/completion paths/hashes | receipt only in deleted journal, completion/routing substitution, witness lock before bundle hash, directory discovery, fixed flat witness file, writer collision/orphan projection |
| Aggregate/material conservation | `452382 = 58089 + 394293`, promotion invariant | aggregate/leaf double count or two material owners |
| Immutable source | pinned Git and checksum-bound asset | branch/tag/local path or changed asset digest |
| Release round trip | full archive format/root/materialization ID/per-asset rights resolves exact bytes | omitted/defaulted root, heterogeneous rights inherited |
| Materialization ledger | acquisition-indexed hash-named sorted/unique JSONL is set-equal to evidence bundle; fixed JSONL is byte-equal projection | unindexed/projection-only receipt, missing/extra/duplicate/reordered receipt, review hash stales byte proof |
| Post-download admission | actual acquired inventory/rights/authorship/labels receive blind decisions and separate source-generation approval before register delta | acquired-only source registered, open inventory, embedded future approval/delta hash |
| License | indexed terms/receipt/scope and approved use | missing, `NOASSERTION`, ambiguous asset/output scope |
| AI evidence | exact generator/model revision/prompt/output/edit binding | alias only, unknown edits, output mismatch |
| Hosted revision exception | official immutable versioning evidence + two blinded accepting decisions/receipt | bare `provider_not_exposed` or pinnable revision |
| Human evidence | pinned benchmark or complete Git history plus independent externally observed exact pre-2020 bytes | Git timestamps alone, negative folder, current repo, absence of AI marker only |
| Family/pair | stable family and same-split pair | unknown family, incomplete pair, pair split crossing |
| Exact/near overlap stream | full 452,382+new persisted rows, bound overlap side, threshold-complete disk join | summary without stream, declared side omitted, LSH-only absence, exact edge `>=0.80` |
| Bounded overlap representation | sharded edges, two-sided adjacency, summary + one-member cluster rows | unbounded `edges[]`/member array, missing reverse edge/member, dense-cluster overflow |
| Real-scale overlap resources | actual bytes/distribution complete within RSS/disk/open-file/wall caps and schema receipt | metadata-only scale, signal/timeout/budget excess, sampled/truncated completion |
| Privacy | zero high-confidence hits | key/token/email/home-path mutation |
| Scaffold/quality | complete parseable target, scaffold <= 50% | truncated/inert target or scaffold-dominant module |
| Review | structured independent role/evidence decisions | bare tuple, same reviewer, missing rights role, hidden disagreement |
| Disposition conservation | every record in one disposition/label cell | omitted/double-counted record; reasons treated as a partition |
| Centralization | one raw source and metadata references | copied AI/human directory trees |
| Census CAS | first-create and replacement lock/transaction survive every mutation/fsync/removal crash | concurrent writer, stale-lock auto-break, unknown-file removal, half-updated pair |
| Acquisition genesis | empty acquisition index generation 0 -> evidence bundle snapshot -> index generation 1 | generation-0 bundle/index fixed point, same/descendant snapshot, direct current write |
| Manifest prerequisite trust | Task 9A receipt schemas + typed staging set/request/publisher completion/current and central kind/owner/path/schema CAS bind the exact Task 9B commit/tarball; build receipts pin immutable bundle/completion/request refs | untyped bare hash, wrong staging member/schema/owner/path, mutable-current historical lookup, platform-root discovery, post-approval package change |
| Manifest publication | ready census/prerequisites -> manifest -> tool/build receipt -> generation -> current, with whole-directory promotion/recovery | receipt embedded in manifest, generation-hash path cycle, flat manifest bypass, stale/two-writer current |
| Determinism | byte-identical ledgers/witness/census generations | mtime/current-time/absolute-path/branch-order perturbation |
| Pull policy | exact Git/release capability, hard materialized/HTTP bounds, honest Git transport status | shell/network-before-census, fake Git transfer cap, proxy/credential/redirect/SSRF, hooks/filters/submodules/LFS |
| Runtime | current Node20-compatible compile plus later packed 22/24 gate | unshipped Node-only API or missing tool behavior receipt |

The artifact linter verifies canonical JSON/JSONL, schema/index coverage,
self-hashes, all referenced files, no absolute host paths, profile/receipt
coverage, exact current register/review equality (329 initially), disposition
conservation, every lock/intended-transaction equality, witness bundle/
publication-completion pair, prerequisite current/bundle/completion/request
chain, and absence of
orphan lock/transaction/temp/transient-handoff files; immutable completed-
handoff twins are required history only for witness/prerequisite/manifest
contracts that bind them, not generic older parents or orphans. The recursive gates run from repository
root after every Task 3B/7/9A/9B code tranche and once again at final handoff; a
focused green test cannot replace its task's full affected-package gates.

Do not call source admission complete when the last command exits 1, even if
millions of raw records are present.

## 13. Completion and stop boundary

Gap 1 is closed when all of the following are true:

1. Every policy/tool-profile/tool-receipt/nested-handoff/source/register/
   generation/current-pointer/evidence/CAS-payload/primary-completion/receipt/
   materialization-ledger/blind-review/temporal/normalizer/overlap/resource/
   privacy/quality/lineage/witness/search/witness-review/census/lock/
   transaction/acquisition and Task 9A/9B prerequisite/manifest contract has a
   Core schema, pure validator,
   mutation tests, and independent approval; runtime context/disposition remain
   SlopBrick-owned.
2. The current evidence normalizes to a byte-reproducible census, including an
   honest initial 0/0 result and conditional controlled 92/92 upper bound.
3. Aggregate/material conservation proves exactly
   `452382 = 58089 + 394293`, while 1,478,350 raw discovery files remain
   separate and promotions do not change additive population.
4. The threshold-complete global overlap universe consumes all 452,382 selected
   legacy rows plus new candidates from the hash-bound record stream, binds an
   authoritative overlap side, uses bounded edge/adjacency/cluster shards, and
   completes on real bytes within the receipt-bound resource envelope;
   unsupported/unreadable/budget-stopped coverage cannot authorize readiness.
5. The initial 329 source reviews equal the initial 329 composed register IDs;
   every later authorized register delta adds its matching review atomically,
   and bounded promotion/review proceeds in order with countable blockers.
6. Public acquisition happens only after a reviewed deficit, explicit
   authorization, and the schema-backed offline-default acquisition CLI; HTTP
   transfer/materialized limits are hard, while Git transport is truthfully
   acknowledged as unbounded or not attempted, and both transports are fully
   origin/address/config isolated.
7. Raw bytes remain centralized once, with no polarity directory duplication.
8. A reviewed census reaches strict 100/100 readiness only through an exact,
   byte-reproducible witness, later acyclic search/blind/witness-review
   receipts, and two independent regenerations, and binds the complete
   verified-context hash set.
9. No manifest, selection, run, or promotion predates that approval.

The source-admission tranche ends at the witnessed approved census. Task 9B is
the separately gated, explicit lossless manifest-builder tranche; Task 10
smoke, Task 11 canary, method freeze, full calibration passes, signal changes,
and release remain later, separately reviewed gates.

## Current execution checkpoint — 2026-07-15

Task 2B is partially implemented at a bounded fixture boundary. The runtime
context now accepts an `independent_review` source only with canonical,
self-hashed source proposal/approval bytes, two blind decisions, a blind-review
receipt, a valid semantic-authority graph, and the generation-local
`source-semantic-authority.json`; genesis-quarantine sources remain
sidecar-free. Candidate-sidecar positive and tamper/missing tests pass **2/2**.
This is not a real-corpus authority and does not advance any admission label.

The non-persisting `census:preview` CLI is parser-strict, canonical-stdout
only, and requires the verified context profile plus exact register/review
selectors. Its 329-source fixture proves canonical output, missing-selector
failure, unknown-option rejection, and no root mutation (**3/3**). The live
v10.3 root still has no static/overlap/witness authority and remains **0
candidate / 0 eligible**, with blockers
`static_authority_unavailable` and `witness_authority_unavailable`.

The planned mutating `rebuild:pre-witness` and
`static-authority:recover` commands are visible but fail closed with
`authority_cli_unavailable` before filesystem access. The fixture-scale
library adapter and nested overlap receipt are not a substitute for the
outer transaction/receipt or the real 452,382-unit run. No repository pull,
label promotion, manifest, release, publish, or deploy is authorized until
that outer graph materializer and recovery path are independently reviewed.

The SlopBrick report writer now uses atomic sibling-temp/rename publication;
watch ignores owned temporary report paths. Brief output labels incomplete
runtime failure separately from policy-threshold failure and includes a
bounded active-rule summary. Renderer/heatmap contracts pass **25/25**,
watch-mode passes **45/45** serially, package typecheck/build pass (with the
existing non-fatal Zod declaration warnings), and `git diff --check` is clean.
The stable recursive workspace gate also passes: Core **226/226**, engine
**59/59**, website **38/38**, and SlopBrick **318 passed / 5 skipped test
files; 3,635 passed / 9 skipped tests**, with recursive typecheck and build
green. Fixture-only stderr remains non-fatal.

These are execution updates, not completion claims. Remaining Task 2B work is
the fully materialized outer rebuild/recovery orchestration, real-scale
overlap/resource receipt, static ledgers, and witness authority; Tasks 3A–11
remain downstream.

## Current Task 2B contract/staging checkpoint — 2026-07-15

The bounded authority boundary has advanced in two separately scoped commits.
The publisher now stages proposal, source-proposal/approval, and
input-generation bytes under a transaction-owned auxiliary subtree, verifies
exact bytes, promotes with no-clobber renames, and cleans only that transaction
after complete or lock-only recovery. Core also exposes a pure builder for the
existing nested-publication handoff: child recovery nonces are derived from
the parent and exact child selector, branch-specific fields are enforced, and
the handoff self-hash is computed and revalidated. Core's 31-file/231-test
gate, typecheck, codegen freshness, contract verification, and build pass;
SlopBrick typecheck and the focused 15-test publication suite pass.

These are contract and fixture-boundary improvements, not real-corpus
admission. The outer graph materializer, parent/child lock and transaction
binding, nested-handoff persistence/recovery, privacy/quality/lineage
builders, real-scale resource receipt, static/witness authority, and full
`rebuild:pre-witness` orchestration remain open. The live corpus is unchanged:
329/329 reviewed sources, 452,382 quarantined or unrepresented units, zero
candidate/eligible units, and blockers
`static_authority_unavailable` and `witness_authority_unavailable`. No
repository pull, label promotion, manifest, release, publish, or deployment
is authorized. The planned commands remain parser-visible and fail closed with
`authority_cli_unavailable` until the fully byte-backed boundary exists.

## Current Task 2B explicit-input/CAS boundary checkpoint — 2026-07-15

The fixture boundary now includes a read-only `preflightAdmissionArtifacts`
helper. It accepts only a complete explicit list of contained
`review/admission/...` paths, checks regular-file bytes, symlink-free
containment, optional lengths and SHA-256 commitments, and returns structured
missing/invalid results without discovery or mutation. Its focused suite is
**4/4**; it is an input-presence diagnostic, not graph, policy, or authority
proof and is not wired to the mutating CLI.

The source-CAS audit is explicit: Core and the loader support exact
content-addressed bundle receipts, but the fixture publisher has no CAS
reservation/reuse transaction. A valid source CAS graph is therefore rejected
before lock creation (**publication 16/16**) rather than copied into a
generation-local directory. This preserves ownership topology until a real
CAS-aware outer materializer exists. The corpus, labels, repository set,
authority trees, and release state are unchanged; Task 2B and all downstream
tasks remain open.

## Allocation before exhaustive row review — 2026-07-15

“Review the corpus” is split into two different gates. Provenance/accounting
coverage must account for every selected unit, but it is an automated join and
does not mean a human must inspect all **452,382** files. The current genesis
register already conserves **58,089** baseline units plus **394,293** repository
units across **329** source IDs. Its `legacy-v5-inventory` row is an aggregate,
open-world inventory view and is deliberately non-additive; the 317 repository
material leaves are the additive owners. The **1,478,350** raw discovery files
are a separate population.

The missing artifact is a row-level allocation ledger. Task 2B's next
implementation slice must consume only explicit, hash-bound inputs: source
register/reviews, pinned repository origin and commit/tree/path identities,
materialization and inventory receipts, rights evidence, and exact
duplicate/overlap joins. It must emit one canonical owner for each selected
unit, or an explicit `unrepresented`/`quarantine` disposition and reason; it
must preserve aggregate rows as non-additive and prove
`452,382 = 58,089 + 394,293`. A streamed/sharded implementation is required
under the existing resource limits; no full corpus load or candidate execution
is allowed.

The ledger can automatically establish origin, ownership, byte identity,
materialization, and overlap coverage. It cannot turn declared AI/human
polarity or an open inventory into `verified_ai`/`verified_human`. Independent
review is still required for authorship, rights/lineage, family/pair leakage,
privacy, and quality, but only a bounded candidate sample should be reviewed
for calibration: smoke **100 positive + 100 negative**, followed by canary
**5,000 + 5,000** from the eligible-gold set. Until the allocation ledger and
its authority inputs are independently approved, counts remain quarantine-only
and no new public repositories should be pulled.
